<pb n="001"/>
<p>śrīrastu ।</p>
<p>bharatamunipraṇītaṃ</p>
<p><q>nāṭyaśāstram ।</q></p>
<p>prathamo'dhyāyaḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>praṇamya śirasā devau pitāmahamaheśvarau ।</l>
<l>nāṭyaśāstraṃ pravakṣyāmi brahmaṇā yadudāhṛtam1 ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 001 !-->
<p>abhinavabhāratī ।</p>
<p>śrīmadabhinavaguptaviracitā vivṛtiḥ ।</p>
<lg><l>yastanmayānhṛdayasaṃvadanakrameṇa</l>
<l>drākcitraśaktigaṇabhūmivibhāgabhāgī ।</l>
<l>harṣollasatparavikārajuṣaḥ karoti</l>
<l>vandetamāṃ tamahamindukalāvataṃsam ।। 1 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>ṣaḍviṃśa(ṣaṭtriṃśa) kātmakajagadgaganāvabhāsa-</l>
<l>saṃvinmarīcicayacumbita1bimbaśobham ।</l>
<l>ṣaṭtriṃśakaṃ <q>bharatasūtramidaṃ</q> vivṛṇva-</l>
<l>nvande śivaṃ śrutitadarthaviveki2 dhāma ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>viśvabījaprarohārthaṃ mūlādhāratayā sthitam ।</l>
<l>dhartṛ3śaktimayaṃ vande dharaṇīrūpamīśvaram ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>sadvipratota4vadanoditanāṭyaveda-</l>
<l>tattvārthamarthijanavāñchitasiddhihetoḥ ।</l>
<l>māheśva<q>rābhinavagupta</q>padapratiṣṭhaḥ</l>
<l>saṃkṣiptavṛttividhinā viśadīkaroti ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>

(mū) 1. pa. yudadīritam ।
(vyā) 1. cumbi । 2. ma. viveka । 3. ma. ka. sarva । kha. dhātṛ । 4. ma. koka ।

<!-- COMMENTARY page 002 !-->
<lg><l>upādeyasya sampāṭhastadanyasya pratīkanam ।</l>
<l>sphuṭavyākhyā1 virodhānāṃ parihāraḥ supūrṇatā ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>lakṣyānusaraṇaṃ śliṣṭavaktavyā2śavivecanam ।</l></lg>
<lg><l>saṅgatiḥ paunaruktyānāṃ samādhānasamākulam ।। 6 ।।</l>
<l>saṅgrahaścetyayaṃ vyākhyāprakāro'tra samāśritaḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>bharatamunirucitadevatānamaskārapūrvakamabhidheyaguṇībhāvena prayojanaṃ mukhyayā vṛttyā
pratijānāno viśeṣaṇadvāreṇa guruparvakramamarthākṣiptatayā cābhidheyaprayojana*tatsambandhānda-
rśayati-- <q>praṇamyetyādinā</q>--</p>
<p>'pitāmaho'tra na pituḥ pitā maheśvaraśca na rājādiriti devaśabdaḥ । etacca
nāśaṅkanīyaṃ prasiddheḥ । eko vijigīṣurnāṭyapravartayiteti devaḥ । bhagavāṃstvānandani-
rbharatayā krīḍāśīlaḥ sandhādau nṛtyatīti nāṭye tadupaskāriṇi ca nṛtte tadupajñaṃ
3pravṛttiriti tāvevātrādhidaivataṃ gurū ceti namaskāryau । lakṣmīpatistu yadyapi vṛttīnāṃ
nirmātā tathāpi pitāmahādivadasau svakartavya4mātraniṣṭhastathācarannātra nāṭye
lokavadupajīvita iti gurutvābhāvanna namaskṛtaḥ ।' (itye)tadapi namaskārahetunirūpa-
ṇasyānucitatvādasat ।</p>
<p>5tasmātpraṇamanaṃ prahvībhāvaḥ kāyena vācā manasā ca । ādyaḥ śiraseti darśitaḥ । 6
dvitīyo devāvityanena । praṇamyasya nirupapadanāmagrahaṇānaucityāt । tena prathamaṃ
devāvityuktam । abhineyaprādhānyāccāṅgikaḥ śiraseti । vācikaśca devāvityādinā
vākyābhinayo darśitaḥ7 । lokasiddho hyayamabhinayo na ca nāṭyadharmirūpaḥ । catura iva
bhujādāvūrdhvādibhinna ityabhineyo8'pi pradarśanīya eva । mānasī tu prahvatā
vākkāyavyāpāragamyeti nāsau pṛthaguktā । 9<q>pitāmahamaheśvarā</q>viti kramaḥ chekānuprāsārthaḥ ।
sālaṅkārasya ca vākyābhinayatāṃ darśayitum । sālaṅkārasya devatāparitoṣahetutvaṃ ca
<!-- APPARATUS page 002 !-->
1 ma. ke vākya । 2. ke muddiṣṭa vaktavyāṅka ।* ke. nāsti । 3. ke. pama. jñaṃ tāṇḍavapravṛtti ।
ka. bhāṇḍapravṛtti । 4. ke. kartavya । 5. ma. praṇāmaḥ kāyādīnāṃ prahvībhāvaḥ । kāyikaḥ śiraseti
darśitaḥ । tasmāt । 6. ke. vāciko । 7. ma.darśitaḥ । kramādetāvāṅgikavācikābhinayau । 8. ma.
anabhineyo'pi । 9. bha. saṃskārasya pūrva buddhau nipatanāccaramasaṃskārasya । pitāmahamaheśvarāviti
krama āśritaḥ । chekānuprāsaparipoṣeṇa sālaṅkārasya ca vākyābhinayatāṃ darśayitum ।
yadvakṣyati--'cekrīḍitaprabhṛtibhirvikṛtaiśca śabdairyuktā na bhānti lalitā bharataprayogāḥ ।' (16-127)
iti sālaṅkārasya ca devatāparitoṣahetutvaṃ darśitaṃ bhavati । prajāḥ prati hitaiṣitvena nāṭyapravartakatvaṃ
kartavyāntaravaikalyena pūrṇatāyāṃ ca tatastadgatatvamiti nāmnorabhiprāyaḥ । tatra nāṭyasya ।

﻿<pb n="003"/>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 003 !-->
darśayitum । pitāmahamaheśvarāvityanena devayorlokahitaiṣitvamuktam । <q>nāṭyaśāstramiti</q> ।</p>
<p>nāṭyasya naṭavṛttasya, śāstraṃ śāsanopāyaṃ granthaṃ pravakṣyāmīti ।</p>
<p>naitadityanye । 'nāṭyavedaḥ nāṭyaśāstram' iti hi paryāyau । tatra nāṭyaśāstra-
śabdena cediha granthaḥ, tadgranthasyedānīṃ karaṇam । na tu pravacanam । taddhi vyākhyānarūpaṃ
karaṇādbhinnaṃ kaṭhena proktamiti yathā । granthasya ca nāṭyavedatve utpattyādipañcakasya
tadgatasyānyagranthasādhāraṇyāt praśnāsaṅgatiḥ । uttaragranthasya cānupapattiḥ- 'dṛśyaṃ śravyaṃ ca
yadbhavet' (1-11) 'jagrāha pāṭhyamṛgvedāt' (1-17) ityādergranthaṃ pratyasaṅgatatvāt ।
tasmānnāṭyaṃ ca tacchāstrañca । vyatputtipradatvāt । tat <q>pravakṣyāmi</q> vyākhyāsye ।
nāṭyākhyaṃ vedaṃ lakṣaṇato nirūpayiṣya ityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>etadapyamanoramam । śabdātmatāvyatirekeṇa pravacanāyogāt । nāṭyasya cāśabdātma-
katvāt । nirūpaṇamātre ca pravacane granthasyāpi pravacanopapatteḥ । nāṭyasya ca procya-
mānatayaivālākṣaṇikabāhyasvarūpanirāsalābhe śāstraśabdānarthakyaprasaṅgāt । 'ya imaṃ śṛṇu-
yātproktaṃ nāṭyavedam' iti śāstrānte yadvakṣyate tasyāsaṅgatyāpatteḥ । śabdaviṣaya-
tātirekeṇa śṛṇuyādityasyāvācakatvāt ।</p>
<p>tasmāditthametaditi <q>madruravaḥ</q> । 'sakalahitakaraṇapravṛtta' 1utsāhasampadopetasta--
dabhivṛddhaye tatpratyūhāpasisāraviṣayā svavijñānakramopārūḍhagururūpa2brahmasarvādhipati--
parameśvaraviṣayā smṛtyautsukyadhṛtimatyādilakṣaṇāṃ vyabhicārasaraṇiṃ bāhyakaraṇīyaviṣayaṃ ca
jaḍatāvahitthaprabhṛtibhāvagaṇaṃ purassarīkṛtya dharmavīrānupraviṣṭastaducitāṅgikavāci-
kānubhāva3 prakaṭanapūrvaṃ svapravṛttiprayojanameva nirūpayati4 । prayojanasyaiva pravarta-
katvāt । yadāhuḥ- 'yamarthamadhikṛtya pravartate tatprayojanam' (nyā. sū. 1-1-24) iti ।</p>
<p>tatra nāṭyaṃ nāma laukikapadārthavyatiriktaṃ tadanukārapratibimbālekhyasādṛśyā-
ropādhyavasāyotprekṣāsvapnamāyendrajālādivilakṣaṇaṃ tadgrāhakasya samyagjñānabhrāntisaṃśayāna-
vadhāraṇānadhyavasāyavijñānabhinna5vṛttāntāsvādanarūpasaṃvedanasaṃvedyaṃ vastu rasasvabhāvamiti6
vakṣyāmaḥ । tasya śāstraṃ śāsanaṃ bāhyabhāṇḍanāṭyādivailakṣaṇyena samyaktatsvarūpāva--
gamopāyaṃ prakarṣeṇa parabrahmaśiṣyodīritānupayogivikāsatvāvadhānena7 (vikāsāvadhūnanena?)</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 003 !-->
1. bha. pravṛtterutsā । 2. sarvabrahmādhi । 3. ke. prakaraṇaṃ । 4. ma. nirūpitavān ।
5. ke. nāṭyābhinna । 6. bha. svabhāveti । ma. rasasvabhāva iti । 7. ma. vikāsabhāvasādhanena ।

﻿<pb n="004"/>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 004 !-->
<p>vakṣyāmi । yadvakṣyati--</p>
<lg><l>ya imaṃ śṛṇuyātproktaṃ nāṭyavedaṃ svayambhuvā ।</l>
<l>kuryātprayogaṃ yaścainaṃ tathā'dhīyīta vā naraḥ ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>yā gatirvedaviduṣāṃ yā gatiryajñavedinām ।</l>
<l>yā gatirdānaśīlānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuyāttu saḥ ।। iti ।।</l>
<l>(............. granthapātaḥ ?) (nā. śā. a. 36)</l></lg>
<p>etena "kāmajo 1daśako gaṇaḥ" (manu. 7-47) iti varjanīyatvena nāṭyasyānu-
pādeyateti yatkecidāśaśaṅkire 2tadayuktīkṛtam । yājñavalkyasmṛtipurāṇādau cāsya
praśaṃsābhūyastvaśravaṇāt । na cāgamādṛte dharmo'numānagamya iti nyāyāt ।</p>
<p>etattu vṛthaivāsthānabhīrūnprati śaṅkāśamanārthamabhidhīyate nāma । tathā hi-naṭānāṃtāva3--
detatsvadharmāmnāyarūpatayā'nuṣṭheyameva । na cāsmākaṃ tacceṣṭitaṃ vicāryam । somakrayo-
padeśino vidhivākyasya na tadvikreṣyad5brāhmaṇāntaragatakṛtyākṛtyavicāraṇodyogo yuktaḥ ।
na cāpyasyopadiśyate 'gāyennṛtyet' iti । kintu prathamanāṭyāvasarakramapravṛttaviriñca--
vacanapravartakabharatamuniśāsanānuvartiśiṣyaparamparāparicayāgatādyatanakālāvadhimahā-
naṭajanasvakapravṛttiviśeṣopadeśaparam । 6ata eva tadgatasiddhisaṃpattisadupāyopadeśana-
paramidaṃ śāstramiti ।</p>
<p>naṭasya tāvannānena kiñcidupadiśyate, taṃ pratyupakārādṛte । kaverapi svahṛdayāyatana--
satatoditapratibhābhidhānaparavāgdevatānugrahotthitavicitrā7pūrvārthanirmāṇaśaktiśālinaḥ
prajāpateriva 8kāmajanitajagataḥ । paraṃ 9pratyāśaṅkā yadi paramatrāvaśiṣyate 10vyutpādyo
varākaḥ । tasyāpi tu neha 'gāyennṛtyedvādayettannirato vā bhavet' ityupadeśaḥ kriyate । api
tu svarasata eva tāvanmanojñaviṣayāsvādapravṛttasyāta eva vedaśāstra--
purāṇādibhīruhṛdayasya tanmanojñavastumadhye tādṛgidaṃ vastvanupraveśitaṃ yadbalādeva pumartho-
pāyāvagatiṃ karotīti vakṣyāmaḥ । utpattyādipraśnāstu ye bhaviṣyanti te nāṭyākhyave--
daviṣayāḥ । na tu nāṭyavedaśāstraviṣayāḥ । yato "nāṭyavedaḥ kathaṃ brahman" (nā. śā.
1-4) ityatra nāṭyameva veda iti vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>etacca nāṭyavedaśāstraṃ brahmaṇodāhṛtaṃ mahyamuktam । yadvakṣyate- "ājñāpito
<!-- APPARATUS page 004 !-->
1. ma. deśako gaṇaḥ । 2. ke tadayukti । 3. ma.bha. naṭasya nāṭyaṃ tāvade । 4. RK hi ।
5. bha. tadvikrayi । 6. ma. bha. paramatadnatasiddhisampattisadu । 7. ma. bha. trāpūrvanirmāṇa । 8. ma. vā
kāma । 9. ma. bha. paramapratyā । 10. ma. ṣyate varākaḥ ।

﻿<pb n="005"/>

<lg><l>samāptajapyaṃ vratinaṃ 1svasutaiḥ parivāritam ।</l>
<l>anadhyāye kadācittu2 bharataṃ nāṭyakovidam ।। 2 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>munayaḥ paryupāsyainamātreyapramukhāḥ purā ।</l>
<l>papracchuste mahātmāno 3niyatendriyabuddhayaḥ ।। 3 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 005 !-->
"viditvā'haṃ nāṭyavedaṃ pitāmahāt । putrānadhyāpayāmāsa" (nā. śā. 1-25) iti ।
atra tu nāṭyasya vedaḥ śāstramiti samāsaḥ । anyathā'dhyāpanāsambhavāt । tena
brahmaproktameva mayā yathāparipāṭi nirūpyata iti yāvat ।</p>
<p>nāṭyaṃ ca brahmaṇoddhṛtyoddhatya vedaṅgānyāhṛtamiti tadviṣayaṃ śāstramapyudāhṛtamityuktam ।
yadi hi nāṭyasya vedanaṃ sattālābho vicāraśca yatra tannāṭyavedaśabdena nāṭyāśrayarūpaṃ
daśarūpakamityucyate-yadvakṣyati "itihāso mayā duṣṭaḥ" iti, (nā. śā. 1-19) ।
atra pakṣe brahmaṇodāhṛtaṃ pradarśitodāharaṇaṃ kṛtanidarśanamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<p>anye tu naṭanīyamanukaraṇaṃ daśarūpakameva nāṭyam । tasyedaṃ śāstram ।
daśarūpakalakṣaṇameva hīdam । 1evaṃ daśarūpakaṃ kavinā kāryam । evaṃ ca naṭanīyamiti
granthātātparyāt । rasādīnāṃ padārthānāṃ tatraiva paryavasānāt । tacca brahmaṇodāhṛtaṃ
kṛtanidarśanam ।</p>
<p>anye tu brahmaṇā vedākhyena bhagavatā śabdarāśinodāhṛtaṃ nirūpitaṃ tyājyānu-
ṣṭheyarūpamāyadāgacchat vyutpādyatayā svīkurvannāṭyaśāstraṃ pravakṣyāmīti prayojanamanenaiva
svīkṛtamityāhuḥ ।</p>
<p><q>bhaṭṭanāyakastu</q> 'brahmaṇā paramātmanā yadudāhṛtamavidyāviracitanissārabhedagrahe
yadudāharaṇīkṛtaṃ 2nāṭyaṃ tadvakṣyāmi । yathā hi kalpanāmātrasāraṃ tata evāna--
vasthitaikarūpaṃ kṣaṇena kalpanāśatasahastrasahaṃ svapnādivilakṣaṇamapi suṣṭhutarāṃ
hṛdayagrahanidānamatyaktasvālambanabrahyakalpanaṭoparacitaṃ rāmarāvaṇādiceṣṭitamasatyaṃ
kuto'pyabhūtādbhutavṛttyā3 bhāti । tathā bhāsamānamapi ca 4pumarthopāyatāmeti । tathā tādṛgeva
viśvamidamasatyanāmarūpaprapañcātmakamatha ca śravaṇamananādivaśena paramapumartha5prāpakamiti
lokottaraparamapuruṣārthasūcanena śāntarasopakṣepo'yaṃ bhaviṣyati ।</p>
<p>'svaṃ svaṃ nimittamādāya 6śāntādutpadyate rasaḥ ।' iti ।। (nā. śā. 6.) tadanena
pāramārthikaṃ prayojanamuktam ।' iti vyākhyānaṃ <q>hṛdayadarpaṇe</q> paryagrahīt । yadāha--</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 005 !-->
(mū) 1. pa. svaśiṣyaiḥ. 2. ga.ma. ttam । 3. N.na.ma.ta. nāṭyavedasamudbhavam ।
(vyā)1 ke. idameva । 2 ke. 3. ma. akṛtākṛtavṛttyā । 4. ma. puruṣārthopadeśopāya । 5. ke.
pravācakamiti । 6. ma. śāntamutpadyate ।

﻿<pb n="006"/>

<lg><l>yo'yaṃ bhagavatā samya1ggrathito vedasammitaḥ2 ।</l>
<l>nāṭyavedaḥ kathaṃ brahmannutpannaḥ kasya vā kṛte ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>3katyaṅgaḥ kiṃpramāṇaśca prayogaścāsya kīdṛśaḥ ।</l>
<l>sarvametadyathātattva bhagavanvaktumarhasi ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 006 !-->
<lg><l>'namastrailokyanirmāṇakavaye śambhave yataḥ ।</l>
<l>pratikṣaṇaṃ jagannāṭyaprayogarasiko janaḥ ।।' iti ।।</l></lg>
<p>evaṃ nāṭyaśāstrapravacanaṃ prayojanamuktam । tatprayojanantu darśitameva । abhidheyaśca
nāṭyavedaḥ । vyutpādyavyutpādakabhāvalakṣaṇaśca sambandhaḥ । yacca śāstra1 yo jijñāsate sa
tāvattadavasare tacchāstrapraṇetari prasiddhe siddhavadeva2 prāmāṇya3mabhimanyata iti 4tadvacano-
ktāya sambandhābhidheyaprayojanāya tadaiva nirviśaṅkaḥ pravartate । parastvadhigatasakalaśāstrā-
rtho bahumanyate na veti tadidamanyat । prathamaṃ tāvatpravṛttamādivākyaṃ 5prayuktameveti svā-
nubhavaprasiddham । tenārthasaṃśayatarkakautukaja(na)nādivākyaṃ pravartakamiti kimanena । (1) ।</p>
<p>6atra muniḥ sakalalokahitakaraṇapravṛttotsāhasaṃpadupeto dharmapīṭhānupraviṣṭastaduci--
tāṅgikavācikānubhāvaprakaṭanapurassaraṃ svapravṛttiprayojanameva nirūpitavān । asya ca
pitāmahamaheśvarau prati smṛtyautsukyadhṛtimattyādayo vyabhicāribhāvāḥ pratīyante ।</p>
<p>atha munirātmānameva paratvena kalpayanbrahmaṇā yadudāhṛtamityetadeva
purākalpapradarśanena niścāyayati-<q>samāptajapya</q>mityādinā ślokadvayenā । anurāgitvaṃ
nāṭyavedayogyatā nāṭyasyāduṣṭatā vinodahetutā sujñānatvaṃ praśnāvasaralābhayogaḥ
prasiddhatvaṃ cācāryayogyatā śiṣṭaprāmāṇikatvaṃ niyamapūrvaśāstragrahaṇaṃ prasiddhādaraṇā-
numeyopādeyatvaprakaṭanamanida7mprāthamyapravṛttatā śiṣyāṇāmūhāpohapāṭavaṃ grahaṇayogyatā ceti
krameṇa padānāṃ tātparyamapunaruktama । (2-3) ।</p>
<p>kiṃ papracchuriti darśayati--<q>yo'yamiti</q> । <q>bhagavatā</q> tatrabhavatā guruṇeti

yacchabdenānirvācyaviśeṣatvamuktam । ata eva na tacchabdasaṅgatiritra mṛgyate8 yathā

<lg><l>[na vedavyavahāro'yaṃ saṃśrāvyaḥ śūdrajātiṣu ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 011 !-->
<p>nanvevaṃ 1tvadharmabāhulyāt sukhameṣāṃ kuta ityāha-<q>devaiḥ</q> śrīmadvijayāvimuktādirudrā--
vatāraiḥ tathā rājasatāmasahṛdaya2janakalṣyamānasaparyākairdānavādibhirākrānte jambūdvīpe ।
devādibhiścākrānte svavaśīkriyamāṇe । nanvevaṃ satsu viśuddhavyāmiśradharmasādhaneṣu kathaṃ
dharmaḥ ? teṣāṃ tatrāpravartamānatvāt । satyam । kintu <q>lokapālaiḥ</q> lokapālāṃśasaṃvibhā--
gasamutpāditaiḥ narapatibhiḥ <q>pratiṣṭhite</q> svadharmasādhanaṃ prati niyojite loke । <q>dṛśyaṃ
śravyaṃ</q> ceti । draṣṭu śrotuṃ cārham । na dharmasādhanam । śakyaṃ ca । na tu durbhaga3paruṣa--
prāyam । loka ityekavacanena sarvasādhāraṇatayaiva yadyogyaṃ tacca spṛśyādirūpaṃ na
bhavati । dṛśyaśravyayostu bahutarasādhāraṇyopapattiḥ । asādhāraṇe cerṣyākrodhādaya eva
pravartante ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati--kṛtayuge sattvapradhāne svadharmamātraniṣṭho loko na sukhaḥduḥkhe prati
heyopādeyadhiyā prayasyati । tretāyāntu rājasattvādduḥkhaṃ jighāṃsati । sukhaṃ ca prepsati ।
rajasaścalatvāt । tadā'sau śāstriteṣu rājaniyantraṇayā pravartyate । tatra ca tādṛgupāyo
nirūpyo yena svayameṣāṃ bhavati pravṛttiḥ । tacca nāṭyameveti ।</p>
<p>cakāreṇedamāha-tādṛśā kenacidupāyena sambandha(ta?)statkurute(stu kṛtaḥ) yena
bhinnendriyagrāhye api dṛśyaśravye ekānusandhānaviṣayatvaṃ na vijahīta iti
sāmānyābhinaya4kālaprāṇatvaṃ prayogasya sūcitam । dṛśyamiti hṛdyaṃ śravyamiti
vyutpattipradamiti prītivyutpattidamityartha iti । anena 5tvi(nanvi)ndrādīnāṃ ka etāvatā
svārthaḥ ? āha । lokapālapratiṣṭhite6 jambūdvīpe gatā ye lokāḥ te hi svadharmāvasthitā
ijyādinā nākamāpyāyayanti । ata evecchāma iti sarveṣāmaikamatyamāha ।
ato'nyonyopakāravṛttyā ca daivamānuṣasargau7 nirūpitau <q>vindhyavāsi</q>prabhṛtibhiḥ । anye
tu svaprayojanameva krīḍā mahendrādīnāmityāhuḥ । tretāyuge pravṛtte evambhūte ca loka
ityanenedamuktaṃ bhavati-- svarge'pi hi tadā tadā mānuṣa8gatarājasadharmābhisambandha--
citritayāgādiyogasarajasīkṛtahṛdayatvāddevā api krīḍanīyakamabhileṣuriti । (10-11)</p>
<p>evaṃ śāstrādhikṛto'pi janaḥ nāṭyena sukhaṃ vinīyata iti prayojanaprayojanamuktvā
prayojanāntaramapyāha--<q>na vedavyavahāra</q> ityādinā । kṛtayuge sattvotkarṣabalādeva sarvaḥ

<p>nanvenaṃ tāvatā niyatānukāro mābhūt । anukāreṇa tu kimaparāddham । na
kiñcidasambhavādṛte । anukāra iti hi sadṛśakaraṇam । tatkasya । na tāvadrāmādeḥ ।
tasyānanukāryatvāt । etena pramadādivibhāvānāmanukaraṇaṃ parākṛtam । na cittavṛttīnāṃ
śokakrodhādirūpāṇām । na hi naṭo rāmasadṛśaṃ svātmanaḥ śokaṃ karoti । sarvathaiva
tasya tatrābhāvāt । bhāve vānanukāratvāt । na cānyadvastvasti yacchokena sadṛśaṃ syāt ।
anubhāvāṃstu karoti । kintu sajātīyāneva । na tu tatsadṛśān । sādhāraṇarūpasya kaḥ
kena sādṛśyārthaḥ । trailokyavartinaḥ sadṛśatvantu na viśeṣātmanā yaugapadyenopapadyate ।
kadācitkrameṇa niyata evānukṛtaḥ syāt । sāmānyātmakatve ko'nukārārthaḥ ।
tasmādaniyatānukāro1 nāṭyamityapi na bhramitavyam । <q>asmadupādhyāyakṛte
kāvyakautuke</q>'pyayamevābhiprāyo mantavyaḥ । na tvaniyatānukāro'pi ।</p>
<p>tenānuvyavasāyaviśeṣaviṣayīkāryaṃ nāṭyam । tathā cāhāryaviśeṣādinā2 nivṛtte
taddeśakālacaitramaitrādinaṭaviśeṣapratyakṣābhimāne viśeṣaleśopakrameṇa ca vinā pratyakṣā3-

camatkārasthānatvāddhṛdayānupraveśayogyatvamabhinayacatuṣṭayena svarūpapracchādanaṃ, prastāvanādinā
naṭajñānajasaṃskārasācivyaṃ, tena rañjakasāmagrīmadhyānupraviṣṭena pracchāditasvasvabhāvena
prākpravṛttalaukikapratyakṣānumānādijanitasaṃskārasahāyena sahṛdayanajñānasaṃskārasacivena
hṛdayasaṃvādatanmayībha5vanasahakāriṇā prayoktrā dṛśyamānena yo'nuvyavasāyo janyate sukhaduḥ--

<p>etadevāha--<q>saptadvīpānukaraṇamayī</q> hi 1kriyā(naṭakriyā)raṅge dṛśyate । na ca

<p>pradhānasya pāṭhyasya pradhānānuraṇanabhūtasya ca gītatodyādervināśaṃ pratipādyābhinaya-

<lg><l>punareva1 hi vakṣyāmi caturaśrasya lakṣaṇam ।</l>
<l>2samantataśca kartavyā hastā dvātriṃśadeva tu ।। 86 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>śubhabhūmivibhāgastho nāṭyajñairnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।</l>
<l>yo vidhiḥ pūrvamuktastu lakṣaṇaṃ 3maṅgalāni ca ।। 87 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>4vikṛṣṭe tānyaśeṣāṇi caturaśre'pi kārayet ।</l>
<l>caturaśraṃ samaṃ kṛtvā sūtreṇa pravibhajya ca ।। 88 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>bāhyataḥ sarvataḥ kāryā bhittiḥ 5śliṣṭeṣṭakā dṛḍhā ।</l>
<l>6tatrābhyantarataḥ kāryā raṅgapīṭhopari sthitāḥ ।। 89 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 065 !-->
<p>yadyapi samacaturaśro'ta eva śakya ūhituṃ tathāpi vispaṣṭārthaṃ vakṣyāmītyāśayena
punaḥ śabdenopakramate--<q>punareveti</q> । nanu vikṛṣṭe stambhavibhāgaṅgayojanādi noktaṃ tatkathaṃ
pratipattavyamityāśaṅkāyāmāvṛttyā'nenaivottaraṃ--caturaśrasambandhi yallakṣaṇaṃ tatpunaryasmādvakṣyāmo
ghaṭasya (yadasya) vikṛṣṭasya sambandhitvena tasmānnāpūrṇaṃ vikṛṣṭalakṣaṇam । tathā yadasya
lakṣaṇamuktaṃ taccaturaśre'pi sañcāraṇīyamiti punaśśabdena darśayati । tenātideśā(śama)--
nāgatāpekṣaṇākhyaṃ tatra yurāti (yojayati) । caturaśramāha--<q>samantata</q> iti । sarveṣvanteṣu
catasṛṣvapi dikṣvityarthaḥ । <q>pravibhajya</q> ceti । pūrvavadevetyarthaḥ । yadi bāhyato bhittirabhyantare
kimityāha--<q>tatrābhyantara</q> iti । aṣṭabhirbhāgaiḥ sarvataḥ kṣetraṃ vibhajet । yena
caturaṅgaphalakavaccatuṣṣaṣṭikoṣṭhaṃ bhavati । tatra madhyamakoṣṭhakacatuṣke raṅgapīṭhaṃ
sarvato'ṣṭahastam । tasya paścime bhāge prākpaścimaṃ dvādaśahastaṃ dakṣiṇottarato dvātriṃśatkaraṃ
tatkṣetramavaśiṣyate । (atra1 yadraṅgapīṭhena svīkṛtaṃ taddhi hastāṣṭakameva ।) yadavaśiṣṭaṃ
kṣetraṃ tanmadhyādraṅgapīṭhanikaṭagataṃ prākpaścimataścaturhastaṃ vistāreṇa dvātriṃśaddhastaṃ
kṣetrāṃśādvibhajya tāvatpramāṇameva paścimabhāge'pi ṣa(ḍdāru)kasaṃsthānaṃ raṅgaśiraḥ kuryāt ।
tato'pi paścime tāvadeva nepathyagrahaṇam(gṛham) । evaṃ sthite raṅgapīṭhaṃ lakṣayitvā daśa
stambhāḥ ṣaḍdārukastambhavyatiriktā deyāḥ । tatra koṇacatuṣṭaye tāvaccatvāraḥ ।
tatrāgneyastambhāccaturhastāntaro dakṣiṇadiśyekaḥ stambhaḥ । tathaiva naiṛ/?/tastambhād dvitīyaḥ ।
<!-- APPARATUS page 065 !-->
<q>ṇa</q>(<q>mū.</q>) 1. ṭha.ma.ta. ataḥ param । 2. ṭha.ma.ta. samantatastu kartavyo hasto । 3. kṣa.
ṭha.maṇḍalāni ca । ma. maṇṭapāni ca । 4. kṣa. ṭha.ma.ba. caturaśrasya tānyeva kārayennāṭyaveśmanaḥ ।
5. ka. śilaṣṭeṣṭakādayaḥ । 6. na. kṛtābhyantarataḥ kāryaṃ raṅgapīṭhaṃ yathāvidhi । kṣa.ṭha.ma.ta. raṅgapīṭhe
yathādiśam । pa. yathā dṛḍham ।
(<q>vyā</q>) 1. bha.ma. ayaṃ raṅgapīṭhena svīkṛtaṃ taddvihastāṣṭaka eva ।

<p>tatra pūrvaraṅgapūrvakatvaṃ prayogakramasya darśayati -- <q>pūrvaraṅga</q> ityādinā । <q>ayamiti</q>

viniyogamasya nirūpayati--<q>pūrvaraṅgavidhā</q>viti । ka(ra)tisthāne raṅge nāṭyaprayoge yaḥ

yatprayuktaṃ taddṛṣṭādṛṣṭobhayaprayojanamapi yathā tatra rañjakatvaṃ kiñcit । anena tu
vimiśraṃ vicitraṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭātmakaphalaṃ samyagvitaratītyabhiprāyo mahāvākyasya ।

1vartanānupraveśo hi śākhayaiva gatārthaḥ syāt tatraiva ca śākhānte bhedaṃ vakṣyati ।

iya(da)meva yuktaṃ karaṇam । na nṛ2 (yannṛ)tyasya pādāgrasthitatvasya kusumāñjalikṣepaḥ ।
sa cānenaiva sampannena caturaśrībhūtatvādaṅgādanantaraṃ yadā prayujyate tadā hastayoḥ sve

9-216) puṣpapuṭaprayogaḥ ।</p>

ityevaṃprakāranṛttahastayojanayā vartitaḥ । cakārādvartanānte "tripatāko'paraḥ karṇe" (nā.śā.
9-199) iti karihastaḥ । pādaśca hastānusāreṇa nikuṭṭitaḥ punaḥ punaranyenāṅgena1 ।
taditi savilāsanṛttaviṣayametat । ata eva lalitaṃ nāma karaṇam । (93)</p>

tadityadhyāhāraḥ ।</p>

iti saptāśītitamam । tataḥ "paryāyaśaḥ kaṭiśchinnā bāhū śirasi" (nā.śā. 4-72)
ityekādaśam ।</p>
<p>ityevaṃ karaṇagrāmasamyagyojanayā kṛtaṃ sthirahastamaṅgahāraṃ nirvartayati । ataḥ(tra)
sarveṣvaṅgahāreṣvityarthaḥ(hāreṣu) karaṇāvayavavargaṃ sarvaṃ karaṇajātaṃ caturdiṅmukheṣu prayojyamiti
nāṭyācāryā manyante । anāgatātītave(dī munistada)yuktaṃ manyamāna ekānnaviṃśatitame
hi parivṛttakarecite'ṅgahāre (nā.śā.4-219) vakṣyati ' parāṅmukhavidhirbhūya evameva
bhavet ' ityaṅgahāravidhāvityarthāyogāt । tadāṅgikeṣveva vakṣyām: । udveṣṭitakaraṇasvarūpaṃ
nirūpayataḥ prayogaścaiṣāmadṛṣṭārtha eva । prayoge ca tattadvā1kyārthādūnaṃ viprakarṣānusāreṇa ।
etacca pūrvaraṅge (a-5) yathopadeśaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ 'yuddhe niyuddhe ca' ityādau (nā.śā.4-56)
viṣayeṇaiteṣāṃ (viśeṣeṇaiteṣām) kadācitprayogaḥ । evaṃ sthirahasta eva nānirva(rtanaṃ) lakṣyata
iti na vṛthā tannirdeśenāyāsaḥ । (176)</p>
<p>(<q>2</q>) <q>paryastakaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>talapuṣpapuṭe</q>tyādi । keci<q>tprasārye</q>tyādinā <q>pratyālīḍhaṃ</q> tataḥ kuryādityantaṃ
sarveṣvaṅgahāreṣu prathamamitikartavyatāṃ yojayanti prathamāṅgasa(ṅga)tikaraṇayogaḥ
kathamityabhiprāyeṇa । anye tu pratyaṅgahārasamucitāḥ sādhāraṇāḥ svayamūhyā ityāhuḥ ।
śrutahānau ko guṇa ityapare ।</p>
<p>tatra "vāme puṣpapuṭa" (nā.śā.4-61) iti prathamam । "āvartya śukatuṇḍākhya--

<q>sannikuṭṭakam</q> । kṣa.ṭha. saṃprasārayet । 5. ḍa.ma. ūruvṛttaṃ tataḥ kuryāduromaṇḍalameva ca । ṭha.tataḥ
kuryādākṣiptasvastikaṃ tathā । kṣa. ūruvṛttaṃ tataḥ kuryāttathaiva ca nikuṭṭakam । 6. na.ma. nitambaḥ

<lg><l>pādasya cānugau hastau trikaṃ ca parivartayet ।</l>
<l>nikuṭya karapādaṃ cāpyuromaṇḍalakaṃ punaḥ ।। 246 ।।</l></lg>
<lg><l>karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kāryamardhanikuṭṭake ।</l>
<l>dvātriṃśadete 1samproktā hyaṅgahārā dvijottamāḥ ।। 247 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 160 !-->
<p>(<q>22</q>) <q>ardhanikuṭṭakaḥ</q> ।</p>
<p><q>kṛtvā nūpurapāda</q>mityādi । "trikaṃ suvalitaṃ kṛtvā-"iti (nā.śā. 4-97)
nūpurapādam । <q>drutamākṣipye</q>tyādinā vivṛttaṃ <q>karaṇamāha</q>--
<lg><l>"ākṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca trikaṃ caiva vivartitam ।</l>
<l>recitau ca tathā hastau vivṛtte karaṇe dvijāḥ ।।" iti (nā.śā.4-122)</l></lg>
<q>nikuṭye</q>tyanane karapādanikuṭṭitaṃ yatra tāni karaṇānyāha nikuṭṭitārdhanikuṭṭakādīni ।
uromaṇḍalakāditrayaṃ pūrvāṅgahāravat ।</p>
<p>ye ye'ṅgahārāsteṣāṃ pratikaraṇaṃ guruparimāṇaṃ kalānivartanakālastāvatā samyakkaraṇaṃ
vartanākrameṇa śakyam । tatra ye ṣaḍdvādaśacaturviṃśa(ti)rityādikaraṇātmakā ekena dvābhyāṃ
vā'bhyasitena yuktāste tryaśramānena boddhavyāḥ । ekasya dvayorvā madhye tu praveśayituṃ
tālakalādyabhisandhānena śakyatvāt । te ca ṣoḍaśātra santi । pūrvavadevāṣṭa--
ṣoḍaśādikaraṇātmakā ekena dvābhyāṃ vā'bhyasitena kiṃcidadhikā vā te caturaśratālaviṣayā
<q>draṣṭavyāḥ</q> । te'pi ṣoḍaśaiva ekasya kvacidūnatve'pi kasyacitpunaḥ kriyayā tālaharaṇaṃ
śakyamiti mantavyam ।</p>
<p>tatrāpaviddha uddhaṭṭito viṣkambhastadapasṛtaḥ svastikarecito vṛścikāpasṛto
mattaskhalito gatimaṇḍalaḥ parivṛttakarecitaḥ parāvṛttako'lātaka udvṛttako recita
ākṣiptarecitaḥ sambhrānto'rdhanikuṭṭakaśceti tryaśratālakāḥ ṣoḍaśa । eṣāṃ
caturaśrāśrayāstāvantaḥ । tatra dvibhedabhinneṣvavāntarabhedena ṣoḍaśasu
pūrvaraṅgāṅgeṣūtthāpanādiprarocanānteṣu bahiryavanikāgateṣu prayogāt dvātriṃśadrūpatetyevaṃ kecit ।</p>
<p>eke tvāhuḥ-- catasṛṇāṃ nartakīnāṃ pratiprayogaṃ catvāra iti punaḥ piṇḍīrecaka-
nyāsāpanyāsaścaturdheti dvātriṃśat । etacca pūrveraṅga(nā.śā.5)vyākhyāne spaṣṭayiṣyāma
ityalam ।</p>

yadā tu nṛttasyādṛṣṭasampādakatve prādhānyaṃ kriyate tadā tadanusāreṇa gītakāderāśrayaṇam ।

drutaṃ caiva" (nā.śā. 4-207) ityaṅgahāre gītakādāvapi madhye strotogatalayādirityādikaṃ

evaṃ śatrujvalanapravṛttāmarṣā(ttasā)bhimānanarapatidvitayavat । ata eva prayujyata ityuktam ।
tenaiva tathākaraṇaṃ sūcyate ।</p>

<p>etadāha--<q>yadā prāptya</q>rthamiti । yato hetorarthānāṃ kāvyārthānāṃ prāptyarthaṃ

<!-- COMMENTARY page 171 !-->
<p>etaddūṣayati--<q>yadā prāptyarthami</q>ti । iha "yo'yaṃ svabhāvo lokasya" iti
(nā.śā.1-119) lakṣaṇena nāṭyaṃ lakṣitam । tatrābhinayānāmupayoga uktārthābhimukhyaprāptiḥ ।
nṛttasya tūktarūpasya na kiñcitprayojanam । uparañjakatayā gītavādyādivadupayoga iti
cet gītasya tāvat--</p>
<p>"yattu kāvyena noktaṃ syāttadnitena prasādhayet ।।" iti</p>
<p>"yāni vākyaistu na brūyāt" iti "na taireva tu vākyārtheḥ" iti nyāyena
prakṛticittavṛttikathāvasthādi sūcayato'styupayogaḥ । vādyasyāpi gītasāmyākṣiptatāloddīpa-
katvena । etanmadhyāttu nṛttaṃ kartṛ kaṃ svabhāvamapekṣate । na yuddhaniyuddhagati-
parikramādāvasyopayoga ityuktam । tatrāpi kaṃ svabhāvaṃ laukikamalaukikaṃ vā'pekṣate ।
laukikatve prayojyatvena lokadharmyā saṅgraho'sya । cārīmaṇḍalādikrameṇa ca tasyāṅga
eva nirūpaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati । athāpyalaukikastathāpi siddham । 'ūrdhvena tu kuryāt'
ityādi caturahastābhinetavyaviṣayavibhāganyāyenābhyadhikaṃ sundaroparañjakabhāgānupraveśena
nāṭyadharmyanupraveśe punarapi nāṭyādabhyadhikatā ।</p>
<p>athocyate--pūrvaraṅgaprayogasya vaicitryasiddhyai tadetaditi । tatrāpi pūrvaraṅgaprayojyayā
brahmagītyā sākam । asyā(thā)ṅgāṅgibhāvena vā । tatrādye pakṣe1 syādasāmañjasyam ।
antye tu pakṣe kathamāhita(ṅgika)hastacāryādyabhāvaḥ ।</p>
<p>taduktam--</p>
<p>"mahāgīteṣu caivārthān samyagevābhineṣyasi ।" iti (nā.śā. 4-15) ।
atrāha--<q>yadā prāptyarthami</q>ti । arthānāṃ gītakapadābhidheyānāṃ prāptyarthamabhimukhaṃ
nayanārtham । yadyayaṃ nṛttābhimato'bhinayo vihitastatkasmādabhinayatve tulye nṛttametanna
nāṭyam । tathāhi--gītakārthābhinaye kartavye kamanyamāṅgikahastakā(cā)ryādya--
bhinayavyatiriktaṃ svabhāvamapekṣate । na kañcidanyamityarthaḥ ।</p>
<!-- APPARATUS page 171 !-->
(<q>vyā</q>) 1. ma. dyapakṣe'sya nāsāmañjasyam ।

<p>athocyate--na gītakādipadārthābhinayatayā'syopayoga iti । kintarhyanyathā
gītakādāvasyopayoga iti । tatrāha--<q>na gītakārthasambaddhaṃ na cāpyarthasya bhāvaka</q>miti ।
iha gītakārthāstadārambhakāḥ vastvaṅgaprabhṛtayaḥ । teṣu na saṃbaddhaṃ tanmadhye na parigaṇitamityarthaḥ ।
yadi hyaṅgavastvādita(va)nmadhyaparigaṇanamasya bhavenna tadbhavedapyanyatadupayogastadārambhakatvāt ।
nacaitadupagatam । na ca yuktam । nṛttasya gītadvitīyajātīyatvāt ।</p>
<p>nanu yathā tatsuṣirādivādyaṃ tadaṅgasambaddhamapi tatropayogi tathedaṃ
bhaviṣyatītyāśaṅkyāha--<q>na cāpyarthasyeti</q> । 1arthyate pradhānatayā gītakādau nirūpyata
ityarthaḥ svarūpapadatālādiḥ । tasyāpyetadbhāvakaṃ prāpakaṃ na bhavati ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati--svarātmake bhāge pratibimbarūpatayā lagnasvaratvena sthānapradāyitayā
svaraparamārthaprāpakatayā svarātmagītibhāge stutaḥ suṣiropayogaḥ । avanaddhasyāpi
tatsāmyopāyatālāṃśaprāpakatvena padapātādabhidheyopayogitve'pyabhinayarūpayā(patayā)
nāṭyādabheda eva syādityuktam ।</p>
<p>athocyate recakāṅgahāranibandhātmakaṃ yannṛttaṃ na tena kaścidartho'bhinīyate । api
tu yathā viśiṣṭairmantraiḥ bhāvanāviśeṣaiścābhyudayasiddhiḥ tathā ।
viśiṣṭadevatāsūcakairmantraistathā tadnīte cābhyadhāyi । gīteṣvāsāriteṣu ceti ।

tatsaṃbandhaścedānīṃ na kiñcit । evaṃ pṛthaṅvṛtta(nṛtta)kāvyādau nāṭyarūpataiva ।

rāgakāvyādinṛttasyeti tadanaikāntika(tva)masya hetoḥ laukikanṛtte'pi sphuṭam ।
nāṭyādilakṣaṇasahagopane tu lokike gātravikṣepaṇaṃ(ṇe) <q>paṭhyamānamabhinīyamānaṃ</q> vā
yāvatpadajātamartho nābhinīyate iti kiṃ nānusandhīyate । kiṃ vā na sākṣātkriyāyogyatāṃ
nīyate । prāpyakalpo'siddhaḥ । loke'pi saumanasyābhāvādaṅgopāṅgaparikṣepānuyātasya
vākyādīritasya dṛṣṭavāt । gīyatā (gāyatā) padārthasaṃvādakṛtatanmayībhāvadagdhā(baddhā)-
yāśca sphuṭameva sāttvikāṅgatāvalokanāt ।</p>
<p>athāparaḥ pakṣastu nṛtte'pi samānam(naḥ) । tathāhi--nṛttakāvye ḍombikādau
varṇacyutādiva varṇādiprayoge tāvadabhinayakathaiva nāstīti kiṃ tatra vicāryate । kevalaṃ

nirṇeṣyata ityāstāṃ tāvadetat ।</p>
<p>tadanantaraṃ tu dhārāparikramapūrvakalayaprayogāvasare "1pāālaalosasāhiṇihujayajaya
ḻacchimaccamaliā" ityādi yadnīyate tatkasyoktirūpam । yadi tāvannartitumāgatāyā
laukikyā ḍombikāpravṛttanartakyāḥ tadā saivedānīmevaṃbhūtaṃ vasturūpaṃ laukikaṃ vacanamabhidhatte ।
gāyanādisvakramikasvavākyata ekavākyataḥ sākṣātkārakalpārthaḥ ।
sākṣātkārakalpānuvyavasāyagocarakāryatvaṃ ca nāṭyasya lakṣaṇamityavocāma ।</p>
<p>tena yathā kaścitkaṃcidanyāpadeśa2gānādikrameṇa vastūdbodhanakaraṇadvāreṇa vā
chandānupraveśitayā vā kasyacinmanasyāvarjanātiśayaṃ vidhatte । nṛtyannapiṃ gāyannapi tadvadeva
ḍombikādau draṣṭavyam । viḍambiḍombityādāvapi (?) vacasi saiva ḍombikā ।
narapatiparitoṣakārthābhidhāyivacananiṣṭhena gītena nṛttena vānyena (vādyena) ca
rājānamanurañjayituṃ gṛhīto mantritvena pūrvaṃ sthitvā madhye kācidīdṛśī
cauryakāmukakelīvāsamanāsādya kāpi punarevaṃvidhā kaścidevambhūtaścauryakāmukaiḥ
ko'pyevambhūtastatra kācidevambhūtā prauḍhadūtītyevamādi rājaputrahṛdayānupraveśayogyaṃ tatprasādena
dhanārjanopāyamabhidadhatī tameva rājaputraṃ paratvena tathaiva vā dhanamuhiśyānyadapi
ceṣṭitamabhidhīyate । ḍombikākṛtyamevopasaṃharati <q>guṇamālāyāṃ</q> "jāmi harārdhātuṃ giapuṇṇaṃ
cisami" ityādau । tatra sā nṛtyatī ḍombikā ca bahutaroparañjakagītādipaṭuceṭakaparivṛtā
tvāṃ pratyevamahamupaślokitavatīti tanmadhyavartigāyanamukhasaṅkramitanijavacanā laukikenaiva
rūpeṇa tadgīyamānarūpakagatalayatālasāmyena tāvannṛtyati । <q>tadnīyamānapadārthasya</q> ca

sātiśayamāvarjanīye rājādau hṛdayānupraveśitāṃ darśayituṃ laukikavyavahāragatahasta--
bhrūkarmaromāñcākṣivikāratulyayogakṣematayaivāṅgavikārādisaṃbhavapyākṣipati ।</p>
<p>evaṃ gītena rañjanaṃ prādhānyena vidhāya tadupayoginaṃ cāṅiganaṃ cāṅgavyāpāraṃ pradarśya
nṛttena punastaccittagrahaṇaṃ kurvatī nṛttaṃ pradhānabhāvaṃ gītaṃ ca tadupasarjanabhāvaṃ nayantī tata
eva tadabhinayamanādriyamāṇā tadgīyamānāṃdbhāvāda/?/kṣiptataduditabhāvamevāṅgavikṣepaṃ karoti
layapariṣvaktakaraṇādau । tatreyatyaṃśe laukikamātasvabhāvarāmanaṭādivyavahāravat kva
prayojyaprayojakabhāvāśaṅkā । kasya vā sāmājikasyaṃ vyutpādanamābhisaṃhitam । tadanantaraṃ
ca yathaiva sā gītanṛttādi prāyuṅkta tathaiva sadṛśaṃ na nartakī prayuṅakte । na tu ḍombikā
sākṣātkārakalpena darśayati tadīyāhāryādinā svātmarūpapracchādanādyabhāvāt । tata eva
na ḍombikāṃ sākṣātkārakalpena sā darśayati । api tu tathaiva nṛttaṃ sābhinayaṃ kevalaṃ
ca pradarśayati tena nāṭyāṅgatāyāṃ yat dṛṣṭaṃ patākādi taddarśanamātratayā। ato nāṭyaṃ
saṃskārakaṃ nṛttasyetyaṅgādivyapadeśa ityupacārāducyate ।</p>
<p>nāṭyasya prastāvanāprāṇapratibimbakalpaṃ nṛttamityayamapi vyavahārastatasya eva ।
nāṭyasyātra nāmāpyasti padamūrdhvādau cāturaśryabhaṅgābhāve (?) tadbhāvādyayogāt
nāṭyarūpatve hi sākṣātkārakalpānuvyavasāyasampattyupayoginaḥ pātraṃ prati bhāṣāniyamasya
chando'laṅkārādiniyamo'vaśa(śya)rūpādyogayogina āhāryaviśeṣasya jātyaṃśakāde(ri)ti
parikramādeśca sa nāsyaivopayoge bhavet । na vaivamasti । mūlabhūtasya ca pāṭhyasya
sambhāvanānuṣaktamākāśabhāṣitamapi syāt । <q>pādatāḍitakādi</q> bhāṇarūpaka iva । iha
tu mūlata eva na kenacitkiñciducyate । "aho gāṇe" tyādi gāyanaṃ yaccoktaṃ "pramadā
saivānukāryātra" iti tadapyanena pratisamāhitaṃ nartakyāḥ svarūpānācchādanāt ।
kalahāntariteyaṃ khaṇḍiteyaṃ nṛtyatīti vyavahāra aupacārikaḥ ।
tadarthagīyamānarūpakagatagītavādyanusāritvāttannṛttasya । na tu mukhyaḥ ।
lambālakatvaveṇīdhāraṇamaṅgalavalayāparigrahāditaducitaveṣādiparigrahavaikalyāt । yacca
nāṭyāyitatvamāśaṅkitaṃ tadasthāne bhrāntam । sahṛdayairnāṭyāyitamiti hi tāvantaṃ
gīyamānamabhinīyate asāṅgatyāpatteḥ । api tu yādṛśā layatālādinā
yādṛgarthasūcanayogyābhinayaḥ sāttvikādipradhānarasānusāritayā prayoga--
yogyastaducitārthaparipūraṇaṃ dhruvāgītena kriyate । sūcyā(kṣmā) hyamī pallavaprakārā
aṅkurādayo nivṛttyaṅkurāntā ye vighnāyitavacca nāṭyāyitam । etacca svakṣetra eva
vitaniṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>evaṃ nāṭyāyitaśaṅkā'pyatra na kācit । mūlabhūtasyābhinayasyaivābhāvāt । tadbhāve
yathā -- muṃcai vaḻavi aṃaa iroaguhaṃsaṇaḻiṇa agni ciṅaja" ityādau

<lg><l>kiṃ tu śobhāṃ 1prajanayediti 2nṛttaṃ pravartitam ।</l>
<l>prāyeṇa sarvalokasya nṛttamiṣṭaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।। 264 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 175 !-->
mūrcchādisākṣātkāraḥ śayyāyāścāṅganipatanādibāhustathā nṛttakāvye'pi syāt । "hośaṃ
daṇaṣaka hamahumāiṣaka" ityādau । nacaivamastītyuktamasakṛt । etena prayojanabhedo'pi
pratyāptaḥ (tyuktaḥ) । nahi sāmājikāḥ prīyantāṃ vyutpadyantāṃ vetyabhisandhinā nṛttaprayogaḥ ।
tatsaṃpattistu nāntarīyakatvādbhavatu । jyotiṣṭomādiprayogasaṅgītāpanodādivadadṛṣṭa-
viśeṣoddeśenaiva hi tasya prayogaḥ । ḍombikāderdṛṣṭoddeśena rājaputrādiprītaye yadyapi
pravṛttirlaukikī sā । adyatve tu na dvayam । nartakyāḥ pravṛttiḥ pravartanā vā
devatāparitoṣaṇaphalaiva । yathoktaṃ tatra--
<lg><l>yatkiñcillāsyametena devastu(vī tu)ṣyati nityaśaḥ ।</l>
<l>yatkiñcittāṇḍavaṃ tena somaḥ sānucaraḥ śivaḥ ।।" iti ।।</l></lg>
mūle ca sūdāderiva vastubhūtarūparasādimadhyapātiviṣayaviśeṣayojanayā kṛtā prītiḥ sādhyā ।
ḍombikāvarṇanagatasyaivālaukikarūpāntaraprādurbhāvāntarasyeti vyutpattyabhisandhānaṃ cānubhavatīti
keyaṃ sambhāvanā geye'pi। nāṭye tu tadeva pradhānaṃ <q>bharatamuni</q>prabhṛtīnāṃ tathaiva 1mūlataḥ
pravṛtteḥ । anyatve tu jīvitā (kā) paryavasitatvaniti puruṣami(ma)tipuruṣadaurātmya--
metaddharmādicatuṣṭayopadeśi purākalpopadeśanamiva pustakavācakānāṃ mūlena pravartanāttatra
vyutpattyabhisandhereveti phalabhedaḥ ।</p>
<p>anyo'pi lakṣaṇabhedo nāṭyarūpatāśaṅkāparakaraṇahetugrantha2vyākhyānāvasare vakṣyate ।
tannāṭyalakṣaṇaprayojanābhedādityasiddho hetuḥ । tadāha nṛttaṃ kartṛ kaṃcidarthamarthyamānaṃ sākṣātkāraṃ
prāpyamānaṃ nāṭyavedaṃ nāpekṣate yena lakṣaṇābhedaḥ syāt । tathā na kaścidarthaḥ
sāmājikānprati vyutpādanīyadharmādyupāyānyatamaṃ vyapekṣate yena prayojanābhedo'pi syādityato
hetoretannṛttaṃ pravartitaṃ nṛttavācoyuktyaiva vyavahṛtam । nanu(tu) nāṭyamiti ।</p>
<p>kiñcidapi śuddhaṃ nāṭyāṅgaṃ pūrvaraṅgādikaṃ veti pāṭho vā iyatā tadanu
prāptyarthamityādi pratisamāhitam । nanu bhavatvevaṃbhūtaṃ nṛttaṃ, nāṭye tu kathamasyopayoga
ityuktaṃ gītakasyāpi kathamupayogaḥ ।</p>

2. kṣa.ḍha.ma. nṛttāmidaṃ stṛtam ।

<lg><l>3vinodakāraṇaṃ ceti nṛttametatpravartitam ।</l>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 176 !-->
<p>uktaṃ-- "yāni vākyaistu na brūyāt" iti" yattu kāvyena noktaṃ syāt"
iti । dhruvāyāstu sampāṭhamātramevāstu । alaṃ varṇālaṅkārayojanātmakagānakriyādi-
prasārāyāsena ।</p>
<p>nanu rāmarāvaṇādigata(tā)grāmyatyājyarūpacaritārthaḍambarasya hṛdayānupraveśadvārabhūtaṃ hṛdyaṃ
tatsūcīkalpaṃ svayaṃ hṛdayānupraveśitvādityuktaṃ prāk । sa eva tarhi nṛttasya
valanāvartanāderantaraṅge'sya nāṭya upayogaḥ । viśeṣato hi tadvinā'lātacakrapratimatve
tairbuddhigrāhyameva nāṭyaṃ na syāt । tata eva vimalābhinayamāṇikyagumphavidhāyisūtrasthānīyaṃ
valanādirūpanṛttasajātīyatvānnikaṭatvādantaraṅgītādivyāpi nāṭyam ।</p>
<p>tadetadāha--<q>kintu śobhāṃ prajanayediti</q> । nṛttaṃ pravartitaṃ prakṛṣṭamatruṭitaṃ
varṇanāvilāsavalanādidakṣiṇaṃ yadvarṇitaṃ kāyāvayavānāṃ kāyasya ca vilāsaceṣṭāvasthānātmakaṃ
vartitaṃ tadātmakaṃ yannuttaṃ tacchobhāṃ rañjanāyogyatvaṃ śobhānāntarīyakacamatkāraṃ prakarṣeṇa
gānādivailakṣaṇyena janayediti nṛttaṃ pravartitamityantenābhisambandhaḥ । hetau liṅ ।</p>
<p>nanu rañjakatvaṃ bhojanādīnāmapyasti । tattadanupraveśanīyamatretyāśaṅkāṃ
madhye'pākarauti--<q>prāyeṇeti</q> । <q>vivāhaprasavāvāhādipu</q> sarvasya lokasya svabhāvataḥ
svabhāveṣvātmābhimateṣu svadehenātmanā nartanamiṣṭaṃ vallabham । sarvo'pi jano svabhāvataḥ
svābhimate vivāhādau nṛtyati yo'pi vādayannṛtyapi tenāpi । durdurūṭenāpi <q>maṅgalyamiti</q>
। <q>vivāho</q> vadhvā ānayanam । tatpūrvakaḥ sarva utsavaḥ । putrajanma <q>prasavaḥ</q> । tato
jāmātuḥ savadhūkasya sarvatra śvaśurabhavanagamana<q>māvāhaḥ</q> । <q>pramodā</q> rājñāmarthakaraṇādayaḥ ।
<q>abhyudayo</q> manorathaprāptirabhilaṣitasyodaya iti । ādigrahaṇenānākāṅkṣitaśubhaprāptyādi
। etena ninimiti (vinodanamiti) ślokatrayasya sambandhaḥ । etacca "kaiśikīmapi yojaya"
(nā.śā.1-42) ityatra darśitam ।</p>
<p><q>kaṃ svabhāvamapekṣata</q> iti pratisamādhātumāha--<q>ataścaiveti</q> । ataśca kāraṇannṛttaṃ
pravartitam । prārambhe pūrvaraṅge lakṣaṇavartitaṃ yojitamiti saṃbandhaḥ । evakāro hetau

(<q>mū</q>) 1. ba. vicārya prasavodvāha । 2. ta. vāvāsa । 3. kṣa. vinodakaraṇaṃ caiva ।

<lg><l>ye gītakādau yujyante samyaṅnṛttavibhāgakāḥ1 ।</l>

yasmātpratikṣepāt । jjhaṇṭumādyāḥ śuṣkākṣarāḥ devaiḥ pratikṣiptatvāt bhūtasaṅghaiśca daityādibhiḥ
pravartitāḥ । (266)</p>
<p>"nirgītaṃ tu savāditramiṃda gṛhṇīmahe vayam ।" (nā.śā. 5-35)

<p>ata evambhūtā gītānāṃ madrakādīnāmādau samyaṅnṛttasyābhineyapadārthābhāve--

prathamatve'bhinayane'syāpi tathāpi tatra na mukhyo nāṭyaprasiddho'bhinayārtha ityuktam ।</p>
<p>kiñcābhineyatvena nāṭyāṅgatvadaśāyāmavalokanāt tathā vācoyuktiḥ ।

<lg><l>vardhamānakamāsādya saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।</l>
<l>kalānāṃ vṛddhimāsādya4 hyakṣarāṇāṃ ca vardhanāt ।। 270 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 181 !-->
hārāṇāṃ prokta iti prakṛtamevānusandhātumāha--<q>tasya taṇḍuprayuktasye</q>ti । tatra
pūrvaraṅgocitatvāyāṅgahāraprayoga ityuktam । tatra ca "tāṇḍavaṃ yatra yujyate ।"
(nā.śā.5-13) iti vardhamānakatāla eva tāṇḍavayogayogya iti pūrvaṃ vardhamānaṃ gṛhṇāti ।
tadanantaraṃ tu gītakādiviṣayo vidhirvakṣyate । <q>tasye</q>ti vyavahitānusandhānārthaḥ parāmarśaḥ
<q>taṇḍuprayukta</q>grahaṇaṃ samanantaroktanṛttakāvyādiviṣayatāṇḍavaśaṅkāṃ nirasyati । vidhīyate'neneti
vidhiḥ gātram । tat dṛṣṭvā yeyaṃ kriyā prayogaḥ saiva lakṣaṇam । anyato
vyavacchedakatvāt । tatra kriyātmakaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmīti sambandhaḥ । (269)</p>
<p>nanu sā kriyoktā karaṇāṅgahāraviṣayā । satyam । gītatālasaṃmiśrā tu noktā ।
iha tu vardhamānākhyaṃ tālamāsādya sāmyāpādanāyopāyatāṃ nītvā tatpramitigītyādhāratvācca
vardhamānaśabdavācyaṃ "devaṃ devaiḥ saṃstutamīśam ।" (nā.śā. 31-98)
ityādivākyasamūhamāsādyābhineyatayāśritya tadākṣiptañca gītaviśeṣamāsādyāṅgasya
valanāvartanādigatadrutatārādiniyamakāritvenāvalambya vakṣyāmīti sambandhaḥ ।
vardhamānakagītatālābhinayasambandhatayoditaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ vakṣyatīti yāvat ।</p>
<p>tatra vardhamānasya bhaviṣyallakṣaṇānuvādena (nā.śā. a-31) tāṇḍavopayogābhidhā-
nāyādyarūpamāha--<q>kalānāmi</q>tyādi । saptadaśakalaḥ kaniṣṭhāsāritakaḥ । sa eva dviguṇalayo
layāntaraḥ । trayastriṃśatkalo madhyamaḥ । pañcaṣaṣṭikalo jyeṣṭhaḥ । tena kalānāṃ layadvāreṇa
saṅkhyādvāreṇa ca vṛddhiḥ। tadvṛdadhyaiva ca hīyamānapadavṛddhirākṣiptā । yadvakṣyati
--"catvārastu gaṇā yugme oje" ityādi (nā.śā. 32-97)। iha tvakṣarāṇi
teṣāṃ vṛddhiḥ kalānusāreṇaiva nartakīnāṃ ca vṛddhiḥ । ekā hi prathamāsārite nṛtte prayoktrī ।
dvitīye dve ityādikrameṇa । ato vṛddhiyogādvardhamānakam । saṃjñāyāṃ kan । kaṇḍikānāṃ
ca daśaparivartakramo bhaviṣyati । prayoge yathā yathākṣaraṃ vinivṛttamityapi yo bhedo bhaviṣyati
tenāpi krameṇa kalādīnāṃ vṛddhiḥ । ato'trāṅgahāraprayogasya paripūrṇasya ca piṇḍībandhavidheḥ
samyaṅniṣpattirbhavatīti tātparyam । (270)</p>

<lg><l>1layasya vardhanāccāpi vardhamānakamucyate ।</l>
<l>kṛtvā kutapavinyāsaṃ yathāvad dvijasattamāḥ2 ।। 271 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 182 !-->
<p>evaṃ lakṣaṇānuvādena tāṇḍavopayogamabhidhāya vidhidṛṣṭāṃ kriyāṃ pratijñānapūrvamāha--
<q>kṛtve</q>tyādi । pūrvaraṅgavidhau vakṣyate--
<lg><l>"kalāpātavibhāgārthaṃ bhavedāsāritakriyā ।</l>
<l>kīrtanāddevatānāṃ ca jñeyo gītavidhistathā ।।" (nā.śā. 5-21) ।</l></lg>
tatra prathamārdhena śuṣkākṣarairāsāritaprayogamāha । tathā ca vakṣyati--
<lg><l>"etāni tu bahirgīte tvantaryavanikāgataiḥ ।।" iti (nā.śā. 5-11) ।</l></lg>
bahirgītaśabdena dvitīyārdhena sārthakapadayuktamāsāritaprayogamāha । tatraiva cocyate--
<lg><l>"tataḥ sarvaistu kutapaiḥ saṃyuktānīha kārayet ।</l>
<l>vighāṭya vai yavanikāṃ nṛttapāṭhyakṛtāni tu ।।"</l></lg>
gītānāṃ madrakādīnām । (nā. śā. 5-12) ityādi ।</p>
<p>tasminnavasare'yaṃ1 nṛttaprayoga iti tamevāvasaraṃ darśayati--<q>kṛtve</q>tyardhena । kutaṃ2 śabdaṃ
pātīti caturvidhamātodyaṃ kutapaṃ tatprayoktṛjātañca । tasya viśeṣaṇa nyāsaḥ vyavasthāpanam ।
tatra viśeṣeṇa nyāso yathāyogaṃ svaratālalayakalādiniveśanam । sa eva
pratyāhārādirāsāritakriyāntaḥ paripūrṇo vinyāsaḥ । āsāritakriyayābhighātātodye
tatprayoktari ca prayokṣyamāṇāsāritagatakalāpātaprastāva evaṃ kriyata ityuktam । sa ca
paripūrṇo vinyāso <q>yathāva</q>cchabdena darśitaḥ । <q>anupūrvaśa</q> iti pāṭhe pratyāhārāvataraṇādyaṅgajātaṃ
sūcayati । tena (e)taduktaṃ bhavati--antaryavanikāgate śuṣkākṣaraprayogaprāṇa--
bhaviṣyadātodyaprayogaprastāvanātmake dṛṣṭaphale daityādiparitoṣaṇayā tadvighnaśamanaśāstrīyaphale
ca prayukte'ṅgakalāpe'yaṃ prayogavidhiḥ । <q>āsāritaprayoga</q> iti sārthakapadaṃ ya ityarthaḥ ।
<q>prayoktṛbhiri</q>tyātodyāntarasāhityaṃ bahuvacanenāha ।</p>

tatthathoktam । <q>gānaṃ</q> suṣirātodyaṃ gīyate yataḥ sthānasvarāditi svarāṇi sādinādīti ।

<lg><l>praṇamya devatābhyaśca tato'bhinayamācaret ।</l>

<lg><l>nṛttāṅgagrāhi vādyajñai1rvādyaṃ yojyaṃ tu tāṇḍave ।</l>

<p>atha vaktavyaṃ sarvaśeṣatvenāha--<q>yadā gītivaśādaṅgami</q>tyādi । mukhyāṅgāni yadā punaḥ

<p>"a(triḥ) nivṛttyā padānāṃ tu māgadhī samudāhṛtā ।" (nā.śā. 32-438) । ityādi ।

<p>"yathākṣaraṃ dvisaṃkhyātaṃ trisaṃkhyātamathāpi ca ।" nā.śā. 31-103) iti । <q>tatreti</q> ।
nivartane । <q>ādyami</q>ti । ādya āvartaḥ । <q>śeṣa</q>mityādi । āvartāntarāṇi
śuddhanuttaprayojyāni । tena na kevalaṃ vastvaṅgādisamāptau nṛttam । yāvanmadhye'pi

tadevaṃvidhameva mantavyam ।</p>
<p>yattu ahaṃ? "jaḻaṇihicuḻui māimā" ityatra, jalanidhiculuke mānitena conmīyata

<lg><l>maheśvarasya caritaṃ ya idaṃ samprayojayet ।</l>

<p>athātra catuṣpadāyāṃ bhāṇḍavādyaviśeṣābhidhānavyājena nṛttasthānaṃ darśayati--
<q>aṅgavastunivṛttau tvi</q>ti । turbhinnakramo'vadhāraṇe । aṅgasyaikasya vā vastuno vā sarvasya

mūhā(?)(pasthāpanā)tmakaṃ1 teṣu prakarṣeṇa bhāṇḍavādyaṃ vaicitryayuktaṃ yojayet । tadvaśācca
tatra nṛttāṅgahārayojanāṃ kuryādityarthaḥ । (317)</p>
<p>atha śuṣkākṣarāyāścatuṣpadāyā vidhirvaktavyaḥ । sā ca pūrvameva prayujyate "āsane-
ṣūpaviṣṭeṣu" ityuktatvāt । ata eva geye gātavye kāvye padamavagamayanta iti
tatpīṭhabandharūpatvaṃ tasyāḥ । tathā cānyatve 2ṣidgakeṣu gātavyātpūrvaṃ tāvatīti nākā-
(re?) । ata eva geye dhruvāgīte geyaṃ gātavyamiti hyeko'rthaḥ । taṃ vidhimāha--<q>ye'pi</q>
<q>cāntaramā</q>rgā iti । antaraṃ parasparavailakṣaṇyaṃ mā3rgyate yenopāyena so'ntaramāryaḥ ।
saṃvādyanuvādinyā4 sa svara upalakṣaṇātmako'rthaprādhānyābhāvācca tenaiva vyapadeśaḥ । ata
evāha tantrīkriyayā vākkriyayā । tade(e)va nirarthakatayā yojitāsteṣu samagrahatvenaiva
bhāva(ṇḍa)prayogaḥ । nartakyā racahādvi(racanāddhi)lāsyāṅgatakāvyārthānusārihastā-
bhinayaśūnyaḥ sāttvikāṅgavalanādimātreṇa sūcyābhinayaḥ । yadvakṣyati--</p>
<p>" vākyārtho vākyavastvaṅgairyojyate yadā pūrvam । " iti । paścādvācā'bhinaya
ityayaṃ tvaṅga ihopalakṣyaḥ । etacca gātavyaprayoge triprakārakṛtatāvanmātra-
tālagānasūcyā'bhinayanamadyāpi dṛśyate ।</p>

<lg><l>evameṣa vidhiḥ sṛ(rdṛ)ṣṭastāṇḍavasya 1prayogataḥ ।</l>

<p>nanvatra pūrvaraṅgagatapradhānaphalenaiva kiṃ phalavattā uta
phalāntaramapyastītyāśaṅkyāha--(maheśvarasyeti) । pṛthakphalavattvaṃ ca daśaryan svātantryeṇa

bhūtvā" ityādyanusāreṇa varṇānāṃ loke prayogaḥ । "tasyāḥ pādāvasāne tu " ityādyanusāreṇa
dhārāparikramādeḥ "yadā gītavaśāt" (nā.śā.4-300) ityanusāreṇa dviguṇādyartha1-
guṇālakavāraṇakaguñjiyakādeścaturapasārakādividhā ca ḍombikādiṣu krameṇa
nartakīvṛddhirācāryairādheyā(?) । tālānusāreṇa ca 'tripāṇilayasaṃyuktam' ityādyanusāreṇa
dhārāparikramādeḥ layapariṣvaṅkitalayatālaparikramādeḥ । (319)</p>
<p>tadetatsarvamīśvaraparitoṣakāryeveti tathaitadupasaṃhārapūrvakamadhyāyāntarāvakāśaṃ karoti--
<q>evameṣa</q> ityādinā । <q>evaṃ</q> pūrvoktena prakāreṇa । <q>prayogata2</q> iti । <q>prayogaṃ</q>
nāṭyātmakamapekṣya tato'nyastadvilakṣaṇo vidhiḥ prakāro <q>dṛṣṭaḥ</q> । tathā nāṭakādisā(dau
sā)mājikavatprayoktṛtanmayībhāvavaśena nāṭyaṃ saṃskāramapekṣyābhinayādividhirdṛṣṭo na tu

pratibimbātmakatā trividhatvānmadamūrcchādau tattvāpattyayogādgītakādeśca niyamādṛṣṭa-

tṛdṛṣṭaphalaprādhānyācca tadvilakṣaṇaṃ nāṭyaṃ tadvṛttirbhidyata iti <q>evaṃ</q> śabdasyārtha <q>ityupādhyāya-</q>
matam ।</p>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 204 !-->
<p>"rasabhāvadṛṣṭihastaśira ādyaṃ yadyaṅgaṃ pūrṇa vā'pūrṇa vā kṛ(ku)ta eva nāṭya-
nṛttayorbhedastulyānukāratve " iti <q>harṣa</q>vārtikam । " śikṣārhasvecchānyanṛttakatipayanāṭ-
yāṅgakṛtaṃ nṛttamabhyāsaphalam । " iti <q>bhaṭṭayantraḥ</q> ।" samayamātramityādimaṅgalavadvivāhādau"
iti <q>bhaṭṭalollaṭaḥ</q> । daśarūpakabhedavallāsyatāṇḍavaprayogo nāṭyabheda eva । tatra
pūrṇānukāra- rūpatvāt ।</p>
<p>tathāhi -praveśe'śvatthāmnaḥ sūcīviddhordhvajānvādi । purūravaso'lapallavasūcī ।
garuḍasya garuḍaplutakam । rāvaṇasya puṣkaro vaiśākharecitakaḥ । vatsarājasyā-
gnisambhramo'(tikrā)ntaḥ । jaṭāyuṣo gṛdhrāvalīnakamelakākrīḍitaṃ ceti "citrābhinayena
bālye(vānye)na karaṇaprayoga eva । abhineyapadādīnāṃ ca nāṭye'pi sakte(ktate)"ti
nāṭyamevedamiti <q>kīrtidharā</q>cāryaḥ ।</p>
<p>etacca (vañca) svamatānusāreṇa <q>evaṃ</q> śabdārthamāhuḥ । yuktāyuktatāṃ tatra parīkṣakā
eva vidurityalaṃ bahunā ।</p>
<p>prasaṅgāṅga(ga)tayā nṛttatayā (vārtayā) prasaktānuprasaktatvena nṛttagatamevānyaktiñcitpra-
siddhiḥ(ddha)prakṛtā(ta)nāṭyagatānāṃ(gatatā mā) vicchedītyabhiprāyeṇāha--<q>nāṭyeti</q> ।

ityarthakrama ādartavyo na khalu śābda iti 5gadanakramānādaraṇaṃ gaditari saṅkramayyoktam ।</p>
<p>tatra pūrvaraṅgaśabdaṃ niruktyā tāvadvyācaṣṭe--<q>pādabhāgā</q> ityādinā ।

<lg><l>1yasmādraṅge prayogo'yaṃ 2pūrvameva prayujyate3 ।</l>

gītakavardhamānādi 1gānaṃ gīyamānaṃ me(ge)yaṃ rūpaṃ saṅgṛhītam । kalāśabdena ca saptavidhā

ca sarūpāṇāmekaśeṣaḥ । <q>pādā</q> ityādi । evaṃ parivartanta iti <q>parivartāḥ</q> । dvisaṅkhyātatri-
saṅkhyātādiṣu, parivartaiḥ sakaletikartavyatā parigṛhītā । cakārātkevalaṃ tantryādi ।
evakāreṇa kevalaḥ prayogaḥ । tathāśabdenāṅgāṅgibhāvaprayogo yathāyogaṃ darśitaḥ ।

ca । tena gītatālavādyanṛttapāṭhyaṃ vyastasamastatayā prayujyamānaṃ yannāṭyāṅgabhūtaṃ sa pūrvaraṅga
ityuktaṃ bhavati । 2yasmādraṅge maṇḍape ādhāre nāṭye vā raṅge buddhisthe bhaviṣyati ।
yujyata eva ca pūrvam3 । pratyāhārādikena hyaṅgena vinā gāyanādisāmagyrasampatteḥ kathaṃ
nāṭyaprayogaḥ । na hyaho (hyeva) kila tantuturīvemādeḥ(vinā) śakyaḥ paṭaḥ kartum । kevalaṃ
prāṅmukhānnabhojanavanni(yamapra)yojanatve'pī(tvamapī)ti vakṣyate । tena pūrvo raṅga iti
pūrvaraṅgaḥ । supsupeti samāsaḥ । rājadantāditvādvā paranipātaḥ।</p>
<p><q>śrīharṣastu</q> raṅgaśabdena tauryatrikaṃ bruvan nāṭyāṅgaprayogasya tasyaiva pūrvaraṅgatāṃ manyamānaḥ
pūrvaścāsau raṅgaśca iti samāsamamaṃsta । yadāha--
<lg><l>"dṛṣṭā ve'vasthārthe nāṭye raṅgāya pādabhā4gāḥ syuḥ ।</l>

<lg><l>kutapasya tu vinyāsaḥ pratyāhāra iti1 smṛtaḥ ।</l>
<l>tathāvataraṇaṃ proktaṃ gāyikānāṃ2 niveśanam ।। 17 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 210 !-->
<p>yathoddeśaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kartumupakramate--<q>eteṣā</q>miti । tatkramamāha--<q>kutapasya tviti</q> ।
nepathyagṛhadvārayormadhye pūrvābhimukho mārdaṅgikaḥ । tasya 1pāṇavikadārdarikau vāmataḥ ।
raṅgapīṭhasya dakṣiṇataḥ uttarābhimukho gāyanaḥ । asyāgre uttarato dakṣiṇābhimukhasthitayo
2gāyanyaḥ । asya vāme vaiṇikaḥ । anyatra vaṃśavāda3kāvityevaṃ kutaṃ pāti kuṃ tapatīti
śabdaviśeṣapālakasya nāṭyabhūmikojjvalatādhāyinaśca vargasya yo vicitro nyāsaḥ <q>sa</q>
viprakīrṇānāmekatra ḍhaukanātmā pratyāhāraḥ ।</p>
<p>yadyapi kutapasya vinyāsamadhya eva ca gāyakasyābhimukhyo raṅgapīṭhasyottarato gāyinya

<p>atha "vighāṭya vai yavanikām" (nā.śā. 5.12) ityādinā
yadgītakavidhyādyaṅgadaśakaṃ darśitaṃ tatkrameṇa lakṣayati --<q>kīrtanādi</q>tyādi । kīrtanaṃ stutiḥ ।

vā । tatra ca tālastālādhyāye (eka)triṃśe vakṣyate । (21)</p>
<p><q>yasmādi</q>ti । tatra pratyāhārīdīni cet atra prayojyāni tatpūrvaraṅga ityanuvādo'yaṃ
syāt । kramasya siddhatvāt । <q>nāndipāṭhakā</q> iti । tadupalakṣitapūrvaraṅgadvāreṇaiva1
purāṇakavayo likhanti sma " nāndyanta sūtradhāraḥ" iti । aharahaścaiṣā prayoge prayojyā ।
eṣā ca nityamevaṃrūpaiva । anyapāṭhyānāmutthāpanādīnāṃ prayogavaśādanyathātvopapattirdṛśyate
। na tu nāndīpāṭhasyeti <q>nitya</q>śabdasyābhiprāyaḥ । <q>ādi</q>grahaṇātprekṣāpatiprabhṛtayaḥ । eṣaiva ca
nāndī bhāratyaṅganirūpaṇe prarocaneti nirdekṣyate--"jayābhyudayinī caiva maṅgalyā" (nā.śā.
20.27) ityādinā । iha tu sā (yā) prarocanā sā tatra bhaviṣyati । atra
nāndīpadānāmantareṣu citre pūrvaraṅge vardhamānaṃ yatprayojyaṃ tatpañcamamaṅgaṃ gaṇayati ।</p>
<p>nanvevaṃ gītakavidhiḥ prathamāṅgānantaramanyāṅgamadhye'pi ca vardhamānaprayogasya citre'pi
bhāvātsaṅkhyāyā anavasthānaṃ na pade'pataditi na punargaṇanārhamiti na doṣaḥ (iti)
kecidāhuḥ । (24)</p>

<p>nanu yadi taiḥ svīkṛtaṃ tataḥ kimityeṣā saṃjñā kṛtā । ata āha--<q>devānāmiti</q> ।

manyāmahe । tathā cedaṃ nābhyantaraṃ bāhyagītamasmābhirgīyata iti tairevaṃ1 veditavyamityarthaḥ ।
(31-41)</p>

roṣitāḥ । 5. ḍa.ma. etannirgītamevaṃ tu ।

<p>nanu nirgītasaṃjñā'sya yā purāṇī tatra kinnimittamityāśaṅkyāha--<q>nirgīta</q>miti ।

iti vacanena gāndharva iva dhruvāgāne parivartānādṛṣṭārthetikartavyatārūpā(patvā)bhāvā1t ।

<p><q>tataśceti</q> । caturaśratālayuktadhruvāyogātparivartanaṃ caturaśram । pādairgīyata iti

<p><q>kāryo nātiprasaṅgaṃ</q> iti । tatraikāṅgahāraprayoga eva kārya ityarthaḥ । ata evā(ṅgā)ntara-
gaṇanayā ṣoḍaśaivāṅgahārāḥ । tathā cotthāpanaṃ parivartanamavakṛṣṭāgānaṃ nāṭyaṃ nāndīpāṭhaḥ
śuṣkāvakṛṣṭajarjaraślokāḥ dhruvā raṅgadvāramaḍḍitā āryāpāṭho dhruvā raudraślokapāṭho narkuṭakaṃ
trigataṃ prarocanā cetyete । aṅgahāraṣoḍaśakameva tryaśre'pīti nāndīpādāntareṣu bahutaraṃ
nṛttam ।</p>

<p>atra hetumāha--<q>bahutvā</q>diti । <q>jñānākhyāni</q> vyākaraṇādīni śāstrāṇi । <q>śilpāni</q>

<p>etadevodbalaya<q>tyekasyeti</q> । nāṭyāṅgabhūtasya kasyaciditi śeṣaḥ । <q>artha</q>syābhidheyasya

<p>saṅgrahādayastvatra sadupāyā iti darśayati--<q>kintviti</q> । nāṭyasya
nāṭyaviṣayasyārthasya <q>saṅgrahaṃ</q> saṃkṣipya gṛhyate'neneti tamuddeśaṃ <q>vakṣyāmī</q>ti । kathaṃ
rasabhāvādi kṛtvā prādhānyāttadupakramamityarthaḥ । kiṃ tenetyāha । <q>anumānaprasādhakaṃ</q> lakṣaṇaṃ

tadupakāriṇyo vṛttayaḥ। dve tisraḥ pañceti nirākaraṇāya <q>catasra</q> ityuktam । tā api
deśavaśādadbhūyasā bhavantīti tadanantaraṃ pravṛttayaḥ। sarvametatsiddhiparyavasānamiti tato dvividhā
siddhiḥ। svarāḥ pāṭhyaṃ gānasaṃgṛhītā api pṛthagupāttāḥ। kevalānāmapi prayogoparañjakatvaṃ
yallakṣye dṛśyate । <q>yatrāntarālāpa</q> iti prasiddhistadabhyupagamārtham । <q>lakṣaṇānvitamiti।</q>
anyattu mallakapaṭaphalakajvālāmukhapakṣavādyādi laukikaṃ naitatsaṅgṛhītaṃ bādhyatvādityarthaḥ।

<p>nanvakruddho'pi naṭaḥ kruddha iva bhāti । satyam । kruddhena sadṛśaḥ। sādṛśyaṃ
ca bhrukuṭyādibhiḥ। 1goriva gavayena mukhādibhiriti naitāvatā'nukāraḥ kaścit । na

<p>evaṃ dvayaprādhānye sarvaprādhānye ca1 codāhāryam । kintu samaprādhānya eva

<p>yadāhuḥ <q>kāvyakautuke-</q>
<lg><l>" prayogatvamanāpanne kāvye nāsvādasambhavaḥ।" iti ।</l>
<l>" varṇanotkalitābhogaprauḍhoktyā samyagarpitāḥ।</l>
<l>udyānakāntācandrādyā bhāvāḥ pratyakṣavatsphuṭāḥ।।"</l></lg> iti ।।</p>
<p><q>anye</q> tu kāvye'pi guṇālaṅkārasaundaryātiśayakṛtaṃ rasacarvaṇamāhuḥ। <q>vayaṃ</q> tu
brūmaḥ-kāvyaṃ tāvanmukhyato daśarupakātmakameva । tatra hyucitairbhāṣāvṛttikākunaipathyaprabhṛtibhiḥ
pūryate rasavattā । sargabandhādau hi nāyikāyā api saṃskṛtaivoktirityādi bahutaramanucitaṃ
kevalaṃ śaktirahitatvādvyāvarṇyate । tāvatīva hyadyamiti nyāyenānaucityaṃ na pratihāri
(na pratibhāti1)। tata evocyate 'sandarbheṣu daśarūpakam (vāmana.kā.) iti । tena tadaṃśa-
(daṅga)sandhyādisaṅghaṭanamuddhṛtya sargabandhādi yāvanmuktaṃ(vatakam)। yattu daśarūpakaṃ tasya
yo'rthastadeva nāṭyam । yadvakṣyate 'nāṭyasyaiṣā tanūḥ'(nā. śā. 14.2) iti tasya
hṛdayasaṃvādatāratamyāpekṣayā śrotṛpratipattṛsphuraṇaṃ sphuṭāsphuṭatvenātivicitram । tatra ye
svabhāvato nirmalamukurahṛdayāstata2 eva saṃsārocitakrodhamohābhilāṣaparavaśamanaso na bhavanti
teṣāṃ tathāvidhadaśarūpakākarṇanasamaye sādhāraṇarasanātmakacarvaṇagrāhyo rasasañcayo
nāṭyalakṣaṇaḥ sphuṭa eva । ye tvatathābhūtāsteṣāṃ pratyakṣocitatathāvidhacarvaṇālābhāya
naṭādiprakriyā । svagatakrodhaśokādisaṅkaṭahṛdayagranthibhañjanāya gītādiprakriyā ca muninā
viracitā । sarvānugrāhakaṃ hi śāstramiti nyāyāt । tena nāṭya eva rasā na loka
ityarthaḥ। kāvyañca nāṭyameva ।</p>
<p>ata eva ca naṭe na rasaḥ। kutra tarhi । vismṛtiśīlo na3 bodhyate । uktaṃ
hi deśakālapramātṛbhedāniyantrito rasa iti keyamāśaṅkā । naṭe tarhi kim ।āsvādano-
pāyaḥ । ata eva ca pātramityucyate । na hi pātre madyāsvādaḥ । api tu tadupāyakaḥ।
tena pramukhamātre naṭopayoga ityalam ।</p>
<p>citrapustādyapi ca nāṭyasyaivārthabhāgābhiṣyando yathā sargabandhādi śabdabhāgābhiṣyandaḥ।
etacca ' yo'rtho hṛdayasaṃvādī । ' (nā.śā. 7.10) ityatra vitatya vakṣyāmaḥ।</p>
<p><q>anye</q> tvabhinayādisāmagrīmayaṃ bahirdṛśyamānaṃ nāṭyaṃ naṭadharmaḥ karma rūpamityāśayena
nāṭyādrasā ityāhuḥ। <q>smṛtā</q> iti sampradāyāvicchedaṃ darśayati । ye tu ratyādyanukaraṇarūpaṃ
rasamāhuḥ atha codayanti śokaḥ kathaṃ sukhaheturiti । pariharanti ca asti ko'pi
nāṭyagatānāṃ viśeṣa iti । tatra codyaṃ tāvadasat । śoko hi pratīyamānaḥ kiṃ
svātmani pratyeturduḥkhaṃ vitanotīti niyamaḥ। śatruduḥkhe praharṣāt । anyatra ca madhyasthatvāt।
uttaraṃ tu bhāvanā vastu svabhāvamātreṇe(tatre)ti na kiñcidatra tattvam ।</p>

<q>(vyā)</q> 1. Kan. 2. T.V. 3. nanu-Kan.

phalaṃ vadhabandhādi । tadvibhāvakenāvaśyaṃ karuṇena bhāvyam । yathā <q>veṇīsaṃhāre</q>--</p>
<lg><l>"adyaivāvāṃ raṇamupagatau tātamambāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā

<p>atha hāsyaṃ lakṣayitumāha--<q>atheti</q> । <q>ātma</q>śabdenedamāha--ratirāsvādanākhyāṃ pratītiṃ

<p><q>atha vīrarasaprakaraṇam</q> ।</p>
<p>kramaprāptaṃ vīraṃ lakṣayati--(<q>atha vīreti</q>) saṃgrāmasamprahārayogo raudre'pīti
vīre'jighāṃseti । ānantarya<q>mathaśa</q>bdenāha । uttamānāṃ prakṛtiḥ svabhāvo yata utsāho'to
vīraraso'pi tathā । yadi vā kāvye nāṭye ca prayujyamāna uttamaprakṛtirheturyasya ।
uttamavarṇānāṃ hi sarvatrotsāha āsvādyo bhavati । ata eva caturṣvapi nāyakeṣu vī-
ratvamanuyāyitvena vakṣyate dhīrodātta ityādi। 2yadyapi sarvo jana utsāhavāneva । 3tathāpi
4tadutsāhasyāviṣayapravṛttatvāttadīyaṃ caritaṃ kāvyanāṭyayornopadeśyam । yadīyaṃ tu
caritamupadeśārha teṣāmucita evāvasare utsāhābhivyaktiḥ । ucitatvaṃ
cāvasarasyāsaṃmohādisampattiriti saiva vibhāvatvenopadiṣṭā । asaṃmohenādhyavasāyo hi
vastutattvaniścaya iti mantraśaktirdarśitā । asadvastvabhiniveśo'saṃmoho rāvaṇādigata
utsāhakārītyasat । aśabdārthatvāt । tatrāpi ca parākramanayādireva vibhāvaḥ।
sandhyādiguṇānāṃ samyakprayogo <q>nayaḥ</q>। indriyajayo <q>vina</q>yaḥ। <q>balaṃ</q> hastyaśvarathapādātam ।

bhāvādhyāye'pi caitadvakṣyate । ārdratāsthāyikaḥ sneho rasa iti tvasat । sneho hyabhiṣaṅgaḥ ।

bhaye viśrāntaḥ । yūnormitrajane ratau । lakṣmaṇādeḥ bhrātari sneho dharmavīra5 eva । evaṃ
vṛddhasya putrādāviti draṣṭavyam । eṣaiva gardha6sthāyikasya laulyarasasya pratyākhyāne
saraṇirmantavyā । hāse vā ratau vānyatra paryavasānāt । evaṃ bhaktāvapi vācyamiti ।</p>
<p>adhyāyārthamupasaṃharan bhāvino'vakāśaṃ dadatsaṅgatiṃ prakaṭīkartumāha--<q>evamete rasā
jñeyā naveti</q> (stvaṣṭāviti)। rasavadgītamityādivyapadeśāt stūyate । sa (śāstu ye te
rasa? mūlā evopacārā iti darśayati--<q>lakṣaṇalakṣitā iti</q> । bhāvānāmapi lakṣaṇaṃ rasa-
lakṣaṇameva pūrayati । vibhāvavyabhicāryanubhāvalakṣaṇena rasalakṣaṇameva pūryate ।
ratisthāyibhāvaprabhavaḥ ṛtumālyādivibhāvako nayanacāturyādyanubhāvaka ityuktamapi
sākāṅkṣameva । kīdṛśī hi ratiḥ kaśca vibhāvaḥ kaścānubhāvaḥ । tena yadyapyāpātato
bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇamidaṃ pratibhāti mahācāryā (sāhacaryāt) tathāpi vākyaikavākyatayā
rasalakṣaṇamevedamityapiśabdasyārtha iti śivam ।</p>
<lg><l>i(ra)tyādiśaktyaṣṭakamadhyavṛttiryasya svahṛnmaṇḍalasamprayojyā(jyaḥ)।</l>
<l>sthāyī śivaścetasi tena vṛttiḥ kṛtā rasādhyāya iha krameṇa ।।</l></lg>
<p><q>iti śrīmahāmāheśvarābhinavaguptaviracitāyāṃ nāṭyavedavivṛtāvabhinavabhāratyāṃ</q></p>
<p><q>rasādhyāyaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ</q></p>
<p><q>samāptaḥ</q></p>

(<q>mū</q>) 1.kṣa.ma. rasavikalpo nāma । ta. rasasvarūpaparipātanaṃ nāma ।
(<q>vyā</q>) 1. parāṅmukhaṃ VR. 2. KLV; rānandānayanaṃ VR. bha. nandanam । 3. ete VR. 4.ma.
pārṣataḥ prasi । pārṣada VR. 5. VR. 6. KA.

<p>śrīḥ</p>
<p>atha saptamo'dhyāyaḥ ।</p>
<p>bhāvānidānīṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ1 । atrāha-bhāvā2 iti kasmāt ।
kiṃ bhavantīti bhāvāḥ3, kiṃ vā bhāvayantīti bhāvāḥ4 । 5ucyate--
vāgaṅgasattvopetānkāvyārthānbhāvayantīti bhāvā iti6 ।</p>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 336 !-->
<lg><l>sthāyī prabuddhahṛdaye vyabhicāribhūtaḥ
kāmākulāsu janatāsu mahānubhāvaḥ ।</l>
<l>antarvibhāvaviṣayo rasamātramūrtiḥ
śrīmānprasannahṛdayo'stu mama triṇetraḥ ।।</l></lg>
<p>bhāvānidānīmiti । nanvadhyāyānta evaitadāsūtritamiti kimanena punaruktena ।
'bhāvāścāpi kathaṃ proktāḥ' (nā.śā. 6-3) ityatraiva praśne kṛte punarihādhyāye 'kiṃ
bhavanti' ityādi ca kimarthamucyate ।</p>
<p>atra kecidāhuḥ- 'bhāvāścāpi' ityadhyāyādau' bhāvānāmapi lakṣaṇam'
itya- dhyāyānte ca vibhāvādīnāṃ sarve(ṣāṃ) sādhāraṇyena praśnapratijñādi । adhunā tu
vibhāvādiṣu vaktavyeṣu prathamaṃ tāvatprādhānyāccittavṛttirūpāḥ sthāyivyabhicāriṇo lakṣaṇīyā
iti tadviṣayaiveyaṃ pratijñā praśnaśca ।</p>
<p>vayaṃ tu brūmaḥ- bhāvaśabdena tāvaccittavṛttiviśeṣā eva vivakṣitāḥ । tathā ca
'ekonapañcāśatā bhāvaiḥ' ityādau tānevopasaṃhariṣyati । teṣāṃ tu yogyatāvaśādyathāyogaṃ
sthāyisaṃcārivibhāvānubhāvarūpatā saṃbhavati । ye tvete ṛtumālyādayo vibhāvā bāhyāśca
bāṣpaprabhṛtayo'nubhāvā ekāntajaḍasvabhāvāḥ te na bhāvaśabdavyapadeśyāḥ ।</p>
<p>nanu rasasaṃvitsvabhāve nimajjanādana evonmajjanācca to'pi saṃvidātmakāḥ । evaṃ
tarhi viśvameva bhāvamayaṃ syādupacārāt vijñānavādāśrayādvetyabhinayadharmyādīnāṃ
<!-- APPARATUS page 336 !-->
(<q>mū</q>) 1. N. kṣa.ka.ca.da. ba.ma. vakṣyāmaḥ । 2. ḍa.ta. bhāva । 3. ḍa.ta. kiṃ bhavatīti
bhāvaḥ । 4. ḍa. kiṃ vā bhāvayatīti bhāvaḥ । kha. kiṃ bhāvayantīti vā । N. kiṃ vā
bhāvayantīti । 5. na. atrocyate । 6.N.omits iti । na.ta. bhāvayatīti bhāvaḥ । bhavati
cātra ślokaḥ । vāgaṅgamukharāgaiśca sattvenābhinayena ca । kaverantargataṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayanbhāva
ucyate ।। bhū iti karaṇe dhātuḥ ।

<pb n="337"/>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 337 !-->
pṛthaktānupapattiḥ । tasmātsthāyivyabhicārisāttvikā eva bhāvāḥ । vibhāvānubhāvānāṃ ca
prāsaṅgikaṃ lakṣaṇam । etacca vakṣyāmaḥ ।</p>
<p>yacca paunaruktyaṃ coditaṃ tadasat । tathā hi -rasādhyāyaprārambhe coditamaṅgamadhye
bhāvā anuddiṣṭā eva kathaṃ tatra tatrodīritā iti । tannirākaraṇārthamāha-<q>bhāvā</q>niti ।
yato'tītādhyāyānte bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ rasalakṣaṇameva ata idānīmapi1 gatacodyāṃśake'vasare
bhāvānvakṣyāmo rasānāmaṅgamadhye paṭhitatvāditi ।</p>
<p>nanu cittavṛttyātmāna eva cedbhāvāstarhyeteṣu vyutpattidvayamapi saṃbhāvyate । tathā
hi 'bhavati'ra2bhūtaprādurbhāve । prakarṣagatiśca punarabhidhānāt । tena3 ye'ntarataḥapūrvatayaiva
prādurbhavati na tu kṣaṇaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate । te(bhyo)4 bhāvāścittavṛttyātmā(no)nubhāvajñānasya
parimitakālabhāvitvāt । yadi vā bhāvayanti āsvādanaṃ kurvanti hṛdayaṃ vyāpnuvantīti5 ।
tataśca vyutpattidvayasaṃbhāvanātkathaṃ 'bhavanti' iti pakṣamanāśaṅkyaiva 'kiṃ vā te bhāvayanti'
iti praśno'yukta ityabhiprāyeṇānudbhinnamarthaṃ praśnasyodbhedayan praśnārthamevānubhāṣate -<q>kiṃ
bhavantī</q>tyādi6 । 7bhavanti bhāvayanti vā । bhāvayantīti ca kimetatkurvanti vyāpnuvanti
vā । tatra ca dvaye'pi kiṃ karma ।</p>
<p>evaṃ praśnārthamanubhāṣyottaramāha--<q>vāgaṅgasattvopetāni</q>tyādi । koḥ kavatervā kavanīyaṃ
kāvyam । tatra ca padārthavākyārthau raseṣveva paryavasyata ityasādhāraṇyātprādhānyācca
kāvyasyārthāḥ rasāḥ । arthyante prādhānyenetyarthāḥ । na tvarthaśabdo'bhidheyavācī ।
svaśabdānabhidheyatvaṃ hi rasādīnāṃ dhvanikārādibhirdaśitam । tacca madīyādeva
tadvivaraṇātsahṛdayālokalocanādavadhāraṇīyam । iha tu yathāvasaraṃ vakṣyata eva ।</p>
<p>evaṃ kāvyārthān rasān bhāvayanti (saṃs?)kurvate । sthāyivyabhicārikalāpenaiva
hyāsvādyo'laukikārtho 8nirvartyate । pūrvaṃ hi sthāyyādikamavagacchati9 tataḥ
sarvasādhāraṇatayā' '10svādayati । tena pūrvāvagamagocarībhūtaḥ sannuttarabhūmikābhāgina

vāgādayastatkarmasu vartante । tena varṇanādyātmanā12 vācikena saṃniveśavalanādinā13-
ṅgikenāntarbahirātmanā sāttvikena karaṇabhūtenopetān sambaddhān ।</p>

(<q>vyā</q>) 1.ma. nīṃ vigata । 2. TV. 3. Kan. 4. Kan. 5. ma. vyāpyānubhavantīti ।
6. ma.bha. kiṃ bhavatītyādi । 7. bha. kiṃ bhavati । 8. KLV. 9. KLV. 10. KLV.
11. KLV. 12. bha. varṇātmanā । 13. ma. dīnāṃ gītenā ।

<p>bhū iti (ṇyantaḥ) karaṇe dhātuḥ tathā ca bhāvitaṃ vāsitaṃkṛtamityana-
rthāntaram1 । 2loke'pi ca prasiddham । aho hyanena gandhena3 rasena vā</p>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 338 !-->
<p>karaṇaṃ hi karmaṇi kartari ca yadyapi saṃbadhyate tathāpi(pī)hāsya prādhānyātsaṃbandhadṛśi
karaṇatvameva darśayituṃ tṛtīyādi(yayā) nirdiśyate1--<q>vāgaṅgamukharāgeṇeti</q> । ata(tra) āhāryaṃ
tu yadyapi nayatkalatādhruvāyātoraṅgamat (nṛtyakalādhruvāpātayorantaraṅgaḥ) tathāpi
tadanantaraṃ cittavṛttyavagatau vācikādīnāmevāntaraṅgatā । tathā hi kāvyādapi rasāsvādo
bhavatītyuktam । tatra ca na pūrṇatā' 'hāryasya । tenāsya nopādānam ।</p>
<p>etaduktaṃ bhavati-cittavṛttaya eva laukikāḥ vācikādyabhinayaprakriyārūḍhatayā
svātmānamalaukikadaśāyāmāsvādyaṃ kurvantītyatastā eva bhāvāḥ । bhavatirhi ṇyantaḥ prakṛtaṃ
karotyarthamāheti darśayati-<q>bhū itīti</q> । ta(ca)kāra uccāraṇārthaḥ । ṇicā saṃbandheneti
ikārapratyaye sati bhūdhātuḥ karotyarthe vartate । etadevopasaṃharati (<q>bhāvitamiti</q>)।
<q>anarthāntaramiti</q> । eko'rtha iti yāvat ।</p>
<p>nanvāsvādyāntarāntarbhāvye vācikādau karaṇamitikartavyatāṃśe vaktavyamityāśaṅkya
tantreṇa vyutpattyantaraṃ darśayan tamāha--<q>loke'pi</q> ceti । na kevalaṃ bhāvitaṃ kṛtamiti
loke prasiddhaṃ yāvadvyāptamityapi । etadapi cetyanenoktam । sarvamityetadgandharasamapi ।</p>
<p>nanu tatrāpi kṛtamityevārtho'stvityāśaṅkyāha--<q>tacca vyāptyartha</q>miti । na hi

ta eva hi vācikādyā abhinayāḥ pramukhadaśāyāṃ deśakālaviśeṣagatatvena yadyapi bhānti
tathāpi naṭasya nirguṇādiha na ta(ṇatvādihata)ttvāt rāmādeḥ 3para(derapara)mārthasattvāt
bhrāntijñānābhāvācca niyatatāṃ vijahataḥ sādhāraṇībhāvamanuprāptāḥ sāmājikajanamapi

ityanarthāntaram । ta. bhāva iti vyāptamarthāntaram । ba. vāsitamiti nāsti । 2. kha.ma.
loke'pi ca siddham । ḍa. loke'pi siddham । na loke'pi ca dṛṣṭam । 3. N.

<lg><l>sarvameva1 bhāvitamiti । tacca vyāptyartham2 । ślokāścātra--</l></lg>

mṛgamadāmodadiśā vyāpnuvanti svacittavṛttivyāpāradvāreṇa । tena bhāvayanti sāmājikā-
tmānamiti bhāvāḥ ।</p>
<p>atha vyutpattyantaramapi darśayituṃ prāktanīṃ ca vyutpattiṃ saṃgrahītumāha-
<q>ślokāścātreti</q> । vibhāvo viṣayaḥ । tena yaḥ āhṛto niṣpāditaḥ । tena vibhāvāpekṣayā
bhāvyate kriyata iti bhāvaḥ । anubhāvānebhyo nirūpayati--<q>vāgaṅgeti</q> ।</p>
<p>anye tu vāgaṅgasattvādyabhinayā yeṣāmiti tadguṇasaṃvijjhānena bahuvrīhiṇā
svābhinayasahitā vyabhicāriṇo gṛhītāḥ । tairiti vyabhicāribhiśca bhāvyate miśrīkriyata
iti vyabhicāriṇāmapi ca vyabhicāriṇo bhavanti । yathā nirvedasya cintā śramasya
nirveda1 ityādi nirūpayanti । taccāsat । sthāyino hi vyabhicāritā bhavati । na
tu vyabhicāriṇāṃ sthāyitā । evaṃ hi sati tadāsvāde rasāntaramapi syāt । yatrāpi
vyabhicāriṇi vyabhicāryantaraṃ saṃbhāvyate tadyathā-purūravasa unmāde'pi tarkacintādi tatrāpi
ratisthāyibhāvasyaiva vyabhicāryantarayogaḥ । sa kevalamamātyasthānīyenonmādena kṛtoparāgaḥ ।

<p>evaṃ lokānusāreṇa kavinaṭaśikṣopayoginā vyutpattyantaramabhidhāya sāmājikābhi-
prāyeṇa yo vyutpattidvayanirūpito'rthaḥ tatsaṃgrahāya ślokadvayamāha--<q>vāgaṅgamukharāgeṇeti</q> ।
vāgaṅgamukharāgātmanā'bhinayena sattvalakṣaṇena cābhinayena karaṇena kaveḥ sādhāraṇaṃ tadāpi-

viṣayajo rāgānta(gassa) eva deśakālādibhedābhāvātsarvasādhāraṇībhāvenāsvādayogyastaṃ
<!-- APPARATUS page 339 !-->

<lg><l>vāgaṅgamukharāgeṇa1 sattvenābhinayena ca ।</l>

<lg><l>nānābhinayasaṃbaddhā2nbhāvayanti rasānimān ।</l>

3atha vibhāva iti kasmāt । ucyate-vibhāvo vijñānārthaḥ4 ।

<pb n="341"/>

<p>1atra ślokaḥ-</p>
<lg><l>bahavo'rthā vibhāvyante vāgaṅgābhinayāśrayāḥ2।</l>
<l>anena yasmāttenāyaṃ vibhāva iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। 4 ।।</l></lg>
<p>athānubhāva iti kasmāt । ucyate--</p>
<p>3anubhāvyate'nena vāgaṅgasattvakṛto'bhinaya iti ।
atra ślokaḥ-</p>
<lg><l>4vāgaṅgābhinayeneha yatastvartho'nubhāvyate ।</l>
<l>5śākhāṅgopāṅgasaṃyuktastvanubhāvastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 5 ।।</l></lg>
<!-- COMMENTARY page 341 !-->
<p>vibhāvenāhṛta ityuktam-tatra yadyapi prakaraṇāccittavṛttyudbhavaheturviṣayo
vibhāvaśabdasyārtha iti jñātam । tathāpi tatra pravṛttinimittaṃ jijñāsamānaḥ tadeva praśnayati-
<q>vibhāva itīti</q>। <q>kasmāt</q> । ṛtumālyādayo'tra vibhāvaśabdena kimiti vyapadiṣṭā iti
bhāvaḥ।</p>

<!-- COMMENTARY page 353 !-->
<p><q>ākārasaṃvaraṇam</q> iti । avahitthe yad bāhulyena dṛśyate tadatrāpīti ।
tadanubhāvayogamāha-yadi vā'vahitthamatra bhavatīti pradarśayatyatra sthāyini śaṅkā
vyabhicāritāmeti tatra niyamenā'vahitthamapīti pradarśyate । na tu vyabhicāriṇi
vyabhicāryantaram । evaṃ hi sati tasminyadanyadityādi śṛṅkhalayā tadādyaṃ vyabhicāritvaṃ
yāyāt । yathā śaṅkāyāṃ cintā, tatrāpi nirvedastatra glānistatrālasyamityādi । evaṃ
sarvatra vyabhicārilakṣaṇa vyabhicāryantaropādānaṃ vyākhyeyam । kecidityanenedamāha- vastu-
saṃvaraṇaṃ kathaṃ śaṅkāṃ gamayatītyāśaṅkyāha-<q>tacca</q> iti । upādhayaḥ saṃvaraṇopāyāḥ
kathāvicchedātikathanādayaḥ । upādhīyate <q>ācchādyate</q> prakṛtaṃ yairiti । upādhīyante'nyatra
prastāve yojyanta iti vā । iṅgitānyaṅgoparispandāḥ sūkṣmā ye saṃvarītuṃ na pāryante,
saṃvaraṇasya ca prāgbhāvinaḥ saṃvivarīpitāste gṛhyante tairupādhyādibhiḥ karaṇabhūtaiḥ kuśalaiḥ
kartṛbhistadākārasaṃvaraṇaṃ śaṅkānubhāvatvenopalakṣayituṃ śakyameva ।</p>
<p><q>dvividhe</q>ti । yadanyairuktamatra dvaividhyaṃ tat sarvavyabhicāriṇāmasti । svātmagato hi
nirvedaḥ kadācit paragato dṛṣṭiceṣṭādyupalakṣyaḥ, ahaṃ nirviṇṇo'yaṃ nirviṇṇa iti pratyayāt ।
tasmādayamatrārthaḥ ātmaśabdena svātmagato'parādhaṃ ucyate, paraśabdena paragato'parādhaḥ । tatra
paragate'parādhe'sambhāvyamāne'pi kutaścinnimittām sambhāvanāpadavīmupeyuṣi yā śaṅkā yathā
<q>nandayantyāṃ</q> darśitā seha parotthā vivakṣitā । etaduktaṃ bhavati । sa eva vibhāvāḥ
svātmani śaṅkā sambhāvyamānadaṇḍanādiviṣayāṃ janayanti । ta eva kadācit
svarūpakarmikāmapi śaṅkāṃ sambhāvyamānadaṇḍānādiviṣayāṃ janayanti । ta eva kadācit
svarūpakarmikāmapi śaḍkāṃ janayanti kiṃ cauro'yaṃ syāditi । nanu tathāpi kathaṃ paratra
cauryādyāśaṅkā jāyata ityāha-<q>dṛṣṭiceṣṭābhiḥ</q> iti । sa hi yadā paraḥ kṛtāparādha
